  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_fcf81cfd-deac-44dc-a577-cbb9742d4e05'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText1588847009170952270" style="display:none">Every story has two sides, and in this new book, the epic love story between Kiera and Kellan is shown through his eyes. <br /><br />All Kellan Kyle needs is his guitar, and some clean sheets of paper. Makes him feel for the first time that <i>he's</i> worth more. But there's one problem— she's his best friend's girl. <br /><br />Just when Kellan thought his emotional defenses were rock solid, Kiera's indecisive heart wreaks havoc on his soul, changing him forever. <a href="/questions/320387-would-i-be-able-to-read-thoughtful-as-a">Would I be able to read Thoughtful as a standalone or would I have to have read Thoughtless for this book to make sense?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_320387'><a id="like_count_community_question_320387" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/320387?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">1 like</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F23200620-thoughtful">like</a></span>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/20853345-rose"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1547990340i/20853345._UY100_CR22,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/20853345-rose">Rose</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Reading Thoughtful alone won't confuse you at all. Everything will make sense. BUT, it's definitely not the same. There are three books and then this <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Reading Thoughtful alone won't confuse you at all. Everything will make sense. BUT, it's definitely not the same. There are three books and then this one which is only the first book in his point of view. If you read only this one, you don't get the full experience. I honestly recommend you read Thoughtless, Effortless and Reckless before reading Thoughtful. I guarantee you'll love it :) <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8047615768413371220"><b> OHHHHH..... MY.... GOD !!!!!!<br/><br/>This is Kellan's POV of Thoughtless!!!! </b><br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413432491i/11509407._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>BLURB: The only place Kellan Kyle has ever felt at home is onstage. Gripping his guitar in a darkened bar, he can forget his painful past. These days his life revolves around three things: music, his bandmates, and hot hookups. Until one woman changes everything…<br/><br/>Kiera is the kind of girl Kellan has no business wanting-smart, sweet, and dating his best friend. Certain he could never be worthy of her love, he hides his growing a</span>
  <span id="freeText8047615768413371220" style="display:none"><b> OHHHHH..... MY.... GOD !!!!!!<br><br>This is Kellan's POV of Thoughtless!!!! </b><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413432491i/11509407._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BLURB: The only place Kellan Kyle has ever felt at home is onstage. Gripping his guitar in a darkened bar, he can forget his painful past. These days his life revolves around three things: music, his bandmates, and hot hookups. Until one woman changes everything…<br><br>Kiera is the kind of girl Kellan has no business wanting-smart, sweet, and dating his best friend. Certain he could never be worthy of her love, he hides his growing attraction…until Kiera's own tormented heart hints that his feelings might not be one-sided. Now, no matter the consequences, Kellan is sure of one thing-he won't let Kiera go without a fight.<br><br>******* TEASER ********<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> She handed me the necklace, and my fingers were shaking as I took it. The guitar was perfectly crafted, delicate, but sturdy, and there was a large circle diamond in the center that sparkled in the lights. It was me, and it was Kiera…the perfect embodiment of what we were, or rather, what we’d never be. I couldn’t think of anything better to give her, to help her remember me, and what we’d gone through. “I’ll take it,” I whispered, not even looking at the price tag.<br><br>“Excellent,” the woman beamed. “I’ll go ring you up.”<br><br>While she walked away, Evan stepped up to me. “Kellan…you can’t expect her to wear that. It’s too obvious.”<br><br>I shook my head as I stared at the glow emanating from the diamond. “I don’t expect her to. I don’t expect anything. But this is what I want to give her.” My eyes were watering when I looked over at him. “This is how I want to say goodbye.”</b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="8047615768413371220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_821141774" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/821141774" />
    <a title="Natalie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4676969-natalie"><img alt="Natalie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551820942p2/4676969.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/821141774?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie" href="/user/show/4676969-natalie">Natalie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24372365-thoughtful">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer821141774" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10442970150601005811"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389539615i/8038831._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>S C Stephens hit the jackpot with this one! <i>Thoughtful </i>is the best book from a male POV I've read. It was even better then <i>Thoughtless! </i>Unbelievable!<br/><br/>One day later, and I'm still recovering from the total mindfuck that <i>Thoughtful</i> was. I had forgotten just how frustrating the Kellan-Kiera-Denny love triangle actually was, and it left me completely drained. But I loved every second of it! Kellan Kyle is worth everything! This is S C Stephens at her best. <i>Thoughtful </i>was everything I ever could have </span>
  <span id="freeText10442970150601005811" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389539615i/8038831._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>S C Stephens hit the jackpot with this one! <i>Thoughtful </i>is the best book from a male POV I've read. It was even better then <i>Thoughtless! </i>Unbelievable!<br><br>One day later, and I'm still recovering from the total mindfuck that <i>Thoughtful</i> was. I had forgotten just how frustrating the Kellan-Kiera-Denny love triangle actually was, and it left me completely drained. But I loved every second of it! Kellan Kyle is worth everything! This is S C Stephens at her best. <i>Thoughtful </i>was everything I ever could have hoped for. Ever since I read <i>Thoughtless</i> years ago, and fell in love with the sexy rock star Kellan Kyle, I've hoping/dreamt that author S C Stephens would write it from his POV. I practically stalked her Facebook page for news daily. But it seemed to good to be true that she actually would.But as it turned out, dreams sometimes comes true. My favourite book (one of,) from my favourite author, from my favorite character' POV, it seemed (again) too good to be true. So when I found out she actually was doing it, my happiness knew no bounds. I've never been this excited for a book realease. Ever! Not in my whole life!<br><br>Can <i>Thoughtful </i>be read as a standalone? Yes. You won't be confused at all. I felt though, that I could enjoy this roller coaster-ride better because I had read <i>Thoughtless </i>first, but it's not a must. If I hadn't, it's fully possible I might have combusted with frustration over Kiera and my heart would have ached so much more for Kellan. S C Stephens really nailed Kellan's POV. She did an amazing job with <i>Thoughtful, </i>Everything we first feel for in Kellan is here, every side of him. And I have never loved him more.I've been waiting years and years to give a book from a male POV 5+ stars, and with <i>Thoughtful</i> I finally can. While I often love the original book, the alternate POV always has been a disappointment. While obviously<i> Thoughtful </i>is a retelling of Thoughtless, it's also so much more. So much that would have stayed a secret is revealed. Conversations aren't simply retold, just the important ones, and many are added. I think than was a brilliant move by the author.<br><br><i>Thoughtful</i> really did a number on my heart. It was a difficult read. My heart ached so much for Kellan.He actually believed that he was useless, worthless and that no one could ever love him.His dreams about his childhood was so hard to read, and the memories haunted him daily. I never hated his parents more. His biggest fear was being alone and yet he was convinced it was his fate.<br><br>Reading Kellan's thoughts were painful but <i>Thoughtful </i>was still a perfect book in its own way. I don't think This instalment was unnecessary at all. It added to the story and especially ones understanding of Kellan. <br><br>I've never felt more connected to Kellan. His thoughts about himself hit me hart, right to the core. They felt so real, and I could actually feel them. Now, more than ever, he has the #1 spot in my heart, forever. I thought I loved him after the three previous books, but my understanding and love for him has grown so much with this book. I really want, no need to read more through his eyes. I need to see him happy, in his thoughts. <i>Thoughtful </i>was so much heartbreak it could last a lifetime. I'm already itching to reread<i> Effortless </i>and <i>Reckless</i>. It's impossible to get too much Kellan!<br><br><i>Thoughtful </i>gave Kellan a whole new, deeper level. If you fell in love with him in <i>Thoughtless, </i>you will love him even more here. Major mindfuck or not-this book made me love Kellan more than ever I love every part of him. Even the parts that hurts to read. Even though it hurts you're my favorite pain.<br><br>What maybe hit me the hardest was the reasons for his many hook ups during the book, his need for meaningless sex. It wasn't the sex itself he craved. It was the connection after. All he ever wanted was for someone to care about him. Not the rock star, just him. <br><br><i>Thoughtful</i> was <b>hot</b>. I might even go so far and say some of the most steamiest scenes was the best ones I ever read. If you have a problem with the hero being with other women, here's a fair warning. I personally had no problem with it what so ever. Why shouldn't Kellan have sex with others? Kiera was the one in a relationship, and she ripped his heart out so many times, Kellan could do whatever he wanted to ease the pain.<br><br><b>Kiera. </b>If you hated her in <i>Thoughtless, </i>you will dislike he even more in <i>Thoughtful</i>. In <i>Thoughtless </i>at least we knew her motives to her every action, but from Kellan's side, she really did seem like a cold bitch and a fucking whore, jumping from bed to bed. I never did hate her in <i>Thoughtless </i>but in this...she really pushed my buttons. She ripped out Kellan's heart more times than I could count and didn't really seem to feel too bad about it. Kellan is a bloody saint for even talking to her.<br><br><b>D-Bags. </b>I can't tell you how good it felt to meet the guys in Kellan's band again. Matt, Evan and Griffin. It was like coming home. Griffin made me laugh out loud every time he was in the book. He is such a funny idiot! It's gonna be so much fun to read Untamed!<br><br>I got a newfound love for <b>Evan. </b>He really was there for Kellan throughout this book. He loved him as a brother and really showed it. I adored the talk between him and Kellan at the hospital. He was one one of my favorite parts of Thoughtful. Griffin too, but that goes without saying.<br><br><b>Denny.</b> I didn't like him him here as much as I did in Thoughtless. don't know why, I still felt a good vibe about him though. It would really be interesting to read his story someday. Here I actually felt like it was Kellan who was the better friend. Strange maybe, considering, but I did.<br><br>The sexual tension between Kellan and Kiera was tangible. S C Stephens is the queen when it comes to that. I'm serious when I say I've never read anything like that before. Kellan loved Kiera so much. Maybe to the point to a little too much. I often felt she was unworthy of his adoration. Kellan was prepared to take every little crumb of love she could give him, he was willing to share her, he just wanted a small part of what she and Denny had. it broke my heart. I feel that Kiera didn't deserve his love. That's one of the reasons I want the rest of this series from his POV so bad. So she can start to make amends to <s>me</s> Kellan. My heart really needs that.<br><br><br><b>| Hero |</b> 5 | <b>| Angst | </b>High focus |<br><b>| Heroine |</b> 5 | <b>| Romance |</b> | High focus |<br><b>| Sexual tension |</b>5 | <b> | Suspense |</b> Low focus |<br><b>| Storytelling |</b> 5 | <b> | Humour |</b> Medium focus |<br><b>| Plot |</b> 5 | <b> | Darkness | </b> Medium focus |<br><b>| Story ending |</b> 5 | <br> <br>**<br><br><i>Acknowledgements<br><br>And lastly, I need to thank Kellan Kyle. You may be fictional, but you completely changed my life, and for that, I owe you everything.</i><br><br><b>#LoveOfMyLife #CanWeGetMarriedPlease #IWantToHaveUrBabies</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10442970150601005811" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer837293708" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8560395391017616156"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426607087i/14066251._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5 Stars for Kellan & Kiera.</b><br/>★★★★★<br/><br/>My Casting:<br/><a href='https://www.pinterest.com/pin/485333297319322202/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kellan</a><br/><a href='https://www.pinterest.com/pin/485333297319322213/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kiera</a><br/><br/>I don't even know how to review this book. Kellen Kyle will always be my number one and that's pretty much the beginning and the end!!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I have a life without you. You’re not my entire world. You’re just the part I loved the most…” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Usually, I just do not have the patience for these alternate POV books. I can't do re-reads and I feel like authors just copy and paste these books, change some of the inner monologues and whack it on Ama</span>
  <span id="freeText8560395391017616156" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426607087i/14066251._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5 Stars for Kellan &amp; Kiera.</b><br>★★★★★<br><br>My Casting:<br><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/pin/485333297319322202/" rel="nofollow noopener">Kellan</a><br><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/pin/485333297319322213/" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiera</a><br><br>I don't even know how to review this book. Kellen Kyle will always be my number one and that's pretty much the beginning and the end!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I have a life without you. You’re not my entire world. You’re just the part I loved the most…” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Usually, I just do not have the patience for these alternate POV books. I can't do re-reads and I feel like authors just copy and paste these books, change some of the inner monologues and whack it on Amazon to get us to part with our money a second time around. And ordinarily, that winds me up. I mean, even with <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> and <i>Hopeless</i>, when I adored the originals, I just felt like I was being conned... <br><br>And to be honest, the same can probably be said for this book. <br><br><i>BUT...</i><br><br>I will never, ever get enough of Kellan. Plus, I think the fact that I read <i>Thoughtless</i> so long ago now, helped so much. I think S.C. Stephens was super smart leaving it so long between books, because there was so much about Kellan and Kiera's story that I'd forgotten and it was like I was reading it for the first time, again.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m in love with you. You gave yourself to me, then ran right back to him. You. Killed. Me.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Whereas, with <i>BD</i> and <i>Hopeless</i>, I felt like their alternate POV books came out pretty quickly, and the story was still fresh in my mind, so I was just going over what I already knew. I don't know if that's the difference, or whether it is simply that S.C. Stephens and Kellan can do no wrong in my eyes. Yes, I know, I totally have double standards. <br><br>But whatever the reason, I fell in love with this story all over again. OMG, the feels!!! Honestly, <i>nothing</i> makes me feel like when I'm reading this series. I love all of the characters so much. These books are so deeply ingratiated into my heart and soul and I really don't think my loyalty to them will ever allow me to love any characters more than them. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Because I was head-over-heels, ends-of-the-earth, till-death-do-us-part in love with her.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>But, if you've read <i>Thoughtless</i> then you know what I'm talking about anyway, so I don't need to harp on. And yes, this review may be a little biased and unfair, but if you love Kellan Kyle as much as I do, and I know many of you do, then hopefully you will feel exactly the same. <br><br>If you haven't read any of this series yet, then I can not tell you how much you need Kellan in your life. You <i>have</i> to read <i>Thoughtless #1</i> asap!!!!! However, in which case, I don't think this book would work so well if you read this too soon after. And equally, if you've only recently discovered this series, this addition might not be for you. However, if you read <i>Thoughtless</i> some time ago and can't remember it word for word, then I think you'll enjoy revisiting with these characters!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389786435i/8054383._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8560395391017616156" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1077606730" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1077606730" />
    <a title="K. Bromberg" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1723129-k-bromberg"><img alt="K. Bromberg" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487968849p2/1723129.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1077606730?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K. Bromberg" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K. Bromberg" href="/user/show/1723129-k-bromberg">K. Bromberg</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1077606730" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17695069515778636433">Just when you thought you couldn't love him more, S.C. Stephens makes you fall in love with Kellan Kyle all over again. In typical fashion, S.C. draws you in, makes you feel like you are part of the story, and then doesn't let you go until the very last page. Emotional, addictive, and a story you'll come back to time and again. Superb!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_819577210" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/819577210" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/819577210?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=love-hate-swingaroo">love-hate-swingaroo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=choke-dat-ho">choke-dat-ho</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=panty-dropping-hot">panty-dropping-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=rock-my-star-bed-house-romance">rock-my-star-bed-house-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer819577210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer953282380448422274"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423624958i/13651894._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='375' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I can’t remember the last time I read something that was purely the alternate POV of the same book…maybe it was Walking Disaster? Hmm I don’t remember, but the point is I don’t read those much because I don’t want there to be a risk of ruining the original version of the story. I took a leap of faith this time because of the hero Kellan Kyle. He’s one of my all-time favorite book boyfriends and there isn’t much I’m not willing to endure while reading if it means he’ll end up in a bette</span>
  <span id="freeText953282380448422274" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423624958i/13651894._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can’t remember the last time I read something that was purely the alternate POV of the same book…maybe it was Walking Disaster? Hmm I don’t remember, but the point is I don’t read those much because I don’t want there to be a risk of ruining the original version of the story. I took a leap of faith this time because of the hero Kellan Kyle. He’s one of my all-time favorite book boyfriends and there isn’t much I’m not willing to endure while reading if it means he’ll end up in a better and happy place. Because honestly? This book had many, many things that would normally drive me up a wall had I read it in another book. <br><br>I also want to say that if you’re reading this book expecting there to be ‘new stuff’ to be added to the original storyline of the Thoughtless trilogy, wrong mentality. When the author said Kellan’s POV of Thoughtless, she <i>really</i> meant that…you’re getting a rehash of book 1 in his view. At this point I would only recommend this book if it doesn’t matter to you that the plot is the same – you just want more Kellan, any way you can get it. I went into this book with that in mind, so my review won’t touch on the plot redundancies, because really, that’s not even supposed to be an issue. <br><br>Now about this book. It was a slow burn, a snooze fest, and an angsty rollercoaster ride all in one. Different sections of the book made me feel different things and by the end, I was just tired and exhausted from it all. First and foremost, reading about Kellan’s heartbreaking upbringing in his own voice downright hurt. The emotional scars his parents left on him were deep, leading him to feel this perpetual loneliness inside of him while on the outside he looked like a perfect golden angel. And yet for all his looks and charisma, he’s insecure about feeling, about emotion, and about love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423624958i/13651895._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Denny and Kiera enter the scene, the snooze fest sort of began. In Thoughtless, part of Kellan’s allure was the fact that I didn’t fully know his thoughts when Kiera did this or that and while it was pretty adorable and heartwarming to see the depth of his love and longing for her, I feel like the author exposed too much if that makes any sense. There are some things best left unsaid, and be open to the reader’s imagination instead, so I was a little discouraged to have to read EVERY single one of Kellan’s thoughts about Kiera this and Kiera that for half of the book. Honestly, these were the parts that drained the life out of me because Kellan’s world IS Kiera. His love for her blinded him to the rest of the world and in everything he does and sees, it’s all her, even when she’s not really his and to have to read about that kind of torment killed me. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423624958i/13651896._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was one thing that really bothered me though, and it was a technical issue so nothing to do with the characters themselves. In my opinion, I think the author is weak with the male POV, and it’s the reason why I can’t bring myself to give this book at least 4 stars. I don’t say this to hurt her; it’s just an observation. Because when I read this book, there really was no difference in writing style or tone between this book and Thoughtless. Kellan must’ve hid his sensitivity very well because in here, he noticed the tiniest things like how eyes have different shades, he used flowery words like ‘blossomed,’ (do dudes really talk like that?), described looks and clothing to the finest detail, etc…all things that I’d normally read from the girl’s POV. <br><br>But in the end, I am glad and immensely thankful that I got to hear his side of the story. Most importantly, it made me understand him better as a person, and though I will always believe Kiera doesn’t deserve him, I now understand why <i>he</i> believes she is the one for him, something I could never accept even though I loved Thoughtless. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423624958i/13651897._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because the plot itself is the same as before, I didn’t feel the same kind of intensity like I did when I read Thoughtless. However, Kellan Kyle himself will stir up enough emotions for you, and if you’re determined to read more about <i>him</i> rather than about the story as a whole, this book will probably be a winner for you.<br><br><u>Thoughtful</u> is Kellan’s POV of <u>Thoughtless.</u> book 1 in the original trilogy. Even though it’s technically a standalone, I would not recommend reading this on its own. At the very least read Thoughtless. <br><br><i>ARC provided by <u>Forever (Grand Central Publishing)</u> via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="953282380448422274" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_854016391" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/854016391" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/854016391?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=cheating">cheating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-rock-god">hot-rock-god</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=1-book-boyfriend-till-the-end-of-t">1-book-boyfriend-till-the-end-of-t</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=number-1-book-boyfriend-till-the-en">number-1-book-boyfriend-till-the-en</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=angsty-read">angsty-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=gutwrenching-and-torturous-read">gutwrenching-and-torturous-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer854016391" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13721857829378711716"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br/>{BR with Mel and Sharon}<br/><br/><br/><b>She was my greatest pain, and my only salvation. She was the only one who could heal this hole in my heart, a hole she'd torn open.</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/8ae6007e140b02bffa84f3ebe23d598c_zpsw2baaejp.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425175082i/13857337._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 8ae6007e140b02bffa84f3ebe23d598c_zpsw2baaejp.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>This was a really hard read for me. I know that I must be just a touch sadistic to have read the series <b>FOUR</b> times, but Kellan truly is my #1 and he's worth the torture. When I finished reading <b>"Reckless"</b> two years ago, I sent an email to S.C. Stephens, just gushing over the book and BEGGING her to write <b>"Thoughtless"</b> o</span>
  <span id="freeText13721857829378711716" style="display:none"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br>{BR with Mel and Sharon}<br><br><br><b>She was my greatest pain, and my only salvation. She was the only one who could heal this hole in my heart, a hole she'd torn open.</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/8ae6007e140b02bffa84f3ebe23d598c_zpsw2baaejp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425175082i/13857337._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8ae6007e140b02bffa84f3ebe23d598c_zpsw2baaejp.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This was a really hard read for me. I know that I must be just a touch sadistic to have read the series <b>FOUR</b> times, but Kellan truly is my #1 and he's worth the torture. When I finished reading <b>"Reckless"</b> two years ago, I sent an email to S.C. Stephens, just gushing over the book and BEGGING her to write <b>"Thoughtless"</b> over in Kellan's POV. I was not ready to let him go. I really wanted to know what was going on in his head during all the turmoil, and where did he go all those times he disappeared for days. Well I definitely got what I wished for. I just am a little sad that the Kellan we get in this one, thinks so little of himself and is filled with so much self loathing. I struggled at times with his inner monologues.<br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Why can't you love me like I love you? Why can't anyone? How awful am I?</b>
</i><br><br><br><br>These self deprecating inner monologues seem to go on for a very long time during the first half of the book. My heart was breaking so much for Kellan. Honestly, I understand why he thought so little of himself. He went his entire life without ever having been loved. I guess that's one of the many reasons I love Kellan so much. He could have turned into a real asshole because of the abuse he endured as a child, but no, he became this incredible guy that gave up his heart and soul for the one woman he truly loved. I just had a hard time with Kellan's self loathing thoughts. I didn't ever remember Kellan being that desperate in the previous books, and I mean, I just reread them this past week.<br><br><br><br><br>I did end up hating Kiera even more in this one. I'm sure there will be plenty of people who will have an even more intense hatred for her. Now that I know how badly she hurt him repeatedly, I am definitely not feeling any sort of sympathy for her.<br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/88aea982e2d47b5de81e9803bbfd3409_zpstiuh9xyn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425175082i/13857338._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 88aea982e2d47b5de81e9803bbfd3409_zpstiuh9xyn.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>The first half of the book, I was feeling so depressed. I was so certain this was going to be a five star read for me, but Kellan being so desperate to take any scraps of attention Kiera would throw his way, really just bugged the ever loving crap out of me. <b>THANK GOD</b> the second half of the book was much better and turned things around for me. Once Kellan stopped being such a door mat, I could breathe a sigh of relief.<br><br><br><br><br>There were some scenes that had me crying like a baby. The "goodbye" song he wrote for Kiera. The talk between Evan and Kellan at the hospital!!! Kellan had a family all along. His band mates loved him like a brother. They were there for him during some of his dark days.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/33f61d9f7650de4300e202f4967e4d9d_zps9u9psu5u.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425175082i/13857339._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 33f61d9f7650de4300e202f4967e4d9d_zps9u9psu5u.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I know sometimes when a book is retold in the other main character's POV, it almost seems like we're just getting the story regurgitated, but I didn't get that feeling at all. I loved experiencing the story through Kellan's perspective and there were plenty of scenes we never got in <b>"Thoughtless"</b>, and man were some scenes very painful to relive in Kellan's POV, like the fight in the rain. <br><br><br><br><br>I'm so happy that S.C. Stephens gave us readers this opportunity to reunite with Kellan and no matter what he will always be my #1. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13721857829378711716" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1082059888" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082059888" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1082059888?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1082059888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13563971041542383907"><a href='http://amzn.com/B00LLIJ1DW' rel='nofollow noopener'>LIVE on AMAZON</a><br/><br/>I don’t think there has been or ever will be another rocker that owns my heart like Kellan Kyle. I still remember all the things I felt while reading <i>Thoughtless.</i> Whether you love or hate it, you have to give credit when I book completely owns you. Thoughtless completely owned me, so while I was <b>terrified</b> to start this one knowing what was going to happen I am glad I did! As I tell my friends, how can you pass up the chance to be in Kellan’s head!<br/><br/>This review will be a little differ</span>
  <span id="freeText13563971041542383907" style="display:none"><a href="http://amzn.com/B00LLIJ1DW" rel="nofollow noopener">LIVE on AMAZON</a><br><br>I don’t think there has been or ever will be another rocker that owns my heart like Kellan Kyle. I still remember all the things I felt while reading <i>Thoughtless.</i> Whether you love or hate it, you have to give credit when I book completely owns you. Thoughtless completely owned me, so while I was <b>terrified</b> to start this one knowing what was going to happen I am glad I did! As I tell my friends, how can you pass up the chance to be in Kellan’s head!<br><br>This review will be a little different since I am assuming if you are reading it you have read Thoughtless, if not please stop since there will be spoilers for the <i>Thoughtless Series</i>. Thoughtful is Kellan’s side of the story and honestly it was so much harder to read. Where Kiera was indecisive and sometimes insensitive, Kellan was heartbreaking. <br><br>My favorite thing about the male POV is seeing how they felt in situations. I love getting into a guys head, I when I read how Kellan reacted to Kiera I was in love. After reading the trilogy, living through the angst, heartache, and tears it is nice to know that there was always something embedded in these two where they were destined to be together regardless. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423876865i/13686235._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know that Kellan was open with Kiera, but reading how he felt when she first walked in. Knowing that his reaction was so much more than a physical reaction means something to me. I know a lot people don’t believe in things like this, but I do. I believe in having a feeling without even knowing why. While I really enjoyed knowing and seeing Kellan’s feelings up front it made for a difficult read, here’s why. <br><br>Throughout the story we are privy to parts of Kellan’s childhood. As you know, his childhood was difficult and ugly, but actually reading some of these scenes just messed me up. Mainly because you see that he carried that stuff into his adult life, his feelings of self worth and self doubt are devastatingly sad. <br><br><b>
  <i>"For the first time in a long time, I was looking at someone who saw me. Not the rock star, not the playboy, but me. The real me."</i>
</b><br><br>That brings me to why this book was so hard to read. First, I love Kellan and while in real life I don’t condone cheating, nor am I an advocate of it, when I read <i>Thoughtless</i> I was screaming “just do it already” - yes I was immediately Team Kyle. So to read <i>Thoughtful</i> and see that her refusal hurt more than his ego and pride, killed me. To see that Kellan was mistreated his whole life, never shown love or affection. Then to know his desire for something real..ugh…bring on the tears. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423876865i/13686236._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I also thoroughly enjoyed getting to see the sexy sneaking around moments from Kellan’s POV, because let’s be honest Kellan Kyle is a ROCK STAR in and out of the bedroom. I love sneaking around, forbidden love, in books and I enjoyed seeing how Kellan planned moments and how they effected him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423876865i/13686237._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Above everything else I loved their love for each other. What can I say, I am sucker for an happy ever after. In the end, things felt complete for me. Seeing both sides, understanding where both people are coming from,it was a full circle moment. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423876865i/13686238._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So my final rating is 4 - 4.5 because there are moments of love, moments of extreme heartache, and moments of rage in this story. Regardless of all that any book that can make me feel so many things is a good book in my opinion. The only reason I can’t give this book a full 5 stars is because there were moments when the story felt long and redundant. However, I do recommend this book, for sure, for readers who loved the trilogy - you really cant pass this one up!<br><br><b>
  <i>You’ll be in my mind every second of every day. I can promise you that. </i>
</b><br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by Grand Central Publishing in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><br>

<span id="freeTextContainer7007452563233143282"><b>4 “I love you Kellan Kyle, even when you look like an obsessed psychopath” Stars. </b><br/>	<br/>I will not dwell on explaining this book's story, because I don’t believe there’s many readers who don’t know Kellan’s and Kiera story. Even the people who didn’t read the books. <br/>Basically, girl moves to another city with boyfriend, they going to live with boyfriend’s friend, boyfriend finds a job in another city, girl and friend fall in love, huge mess happens. (In a very short way, it’s basically it).<br/>We’ve read </span>
  <span id="freeText7007452563233143282" style="display:none"><b>4 “I love you Kellan Kyle, even when you look like an obsessed psychopath” Stars. </b><br>	<br>I will not dwell on explaining this book's story, because I don’t believe there’s many readers who don’t know Kellan’s and Kiera story. Even the people who didn’t read the books. <br>Basically, girl moves to another city with boyfriend, they going to live with boyfriend’s friend, boyfriend finds a job in another city, girl and friend fall in love, huge mess happens. (In a very short way, it’s basically it).<br>We’ve read this story trough Kiera’s eyes, but in this book it was Kellan’s time to tell the story. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424902395i/13817812.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Despite not being necessary, I advise you to read this book only if you have read the “Thoughtless” series before. And if you haven’t, get on it, like… yesterday. <br>If for some reason you want to break something after reading the first book, don’t give up… the two others after that are perfection. <br>Maybe it’s because I already know how this ends, but reading this wasn’t as hard as it was “Thoughtless”. Still, it was angsty, emotional and when it ended I had go read “Reckless” epilogue just to remember exactly how this whole mess ended. <br>This series was one of my favorites ever and it was great to be inside Kellan’s mind, even when he looked a little nuts. If you’re a fan of the series you can’t miss this book. <br>(On another note… I know that Reckless already has one, but it would kill give us another epilogue? Maybe one further in time?) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422226870i/13474212.jpg" width="350" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> If I haven’t read the whole trilogy before, I would have loathed Kiera. And in some moments, I did. Luckily I know she gets better and ends up redeeming from all of this mess, so I got over it. Kellan is a different story, he’s a book-boyfriend I’ll always love, but seeing this story trough this eyes, not only was hard, as in some moments he was so obsessed over Kiera that he looked borderline psychopath. Being inside his mind was painful at several moments, but I loved this opportunity for being there. I loved seeing the D-Bags trough his eyes and the friendship between them and I had almost forgotten how I loved Anna! It was nice to see more of her, either. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Some hot scenes. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Besides Kellan f*cked up past and mind? Not really… <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/823414667" />
    <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance"><img alt="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481665315p2/10247668.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823414667?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=rockstar">rockstar</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=top-favourite-reads-of-all-time">top-favourite-reads-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=conquer-my-tbr-in-2015">conquer-my-tbr-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823414667" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8869865395791643352"><b>3.75 I'm so very sorry and I feel very guilty about this stars***</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/42FDA7AA-2226-43C9-AEA8-2A9CFA92B7EC_zpsz1gls1vu.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425332990i/13878312._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 42FDA7AA-2226-43C9-AEA8-2A9CFA92B7EC_zpsz1gls1vu.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> <br/>Three years ago I had a baby.<br/>Three years ago I had a baby that fed continuously through the night.<br/>Three years ago I started to read again.<br/>Three years ago I fell for Kellan Kyle.<br/>Three years ago I stayed up till 4am reading thoughtless then 5am with Effortless.<br/>And Three years later I read Thoughtful in <b>TWO LONG WEEKS</b> even after staying up late reading!! <br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>" I dream about you sometimes... about what it would have been like if De</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText8869865395791643352" style="display:none"><b>3.75 I'm so very sorry and I feel very guilty about this stars***</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/42FDA7AA-2226-43C9-AEA8-2A9CFA92B7EC_zpsz1gls1vu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425332990i/13878312._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 42FDA7AA-2226-43C9-AEA8-2A9CFA92B7EC_zpsz1gls1vu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Three years ago I had a baby.<br>Three years ago I had a baby that fed continuously through the night.<br>Three years ago I started to read again.<br>Three years ago I fell for Kellan Kyle.<br>Three years ago I stayed up till 4am reading thoughtless then 5am with Effortless.<br>And Three years later I read Thoughtful in <b>TWO LONG WEEKS</b> even after staying up late reading!! <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>" I dream about you sometimes... about what it would have been like if Denny hadn't come back, if you were mine. Holding your hand, walking into the bar with you on my arm.... not having to hide anything anymore. Telling the world that I love you."</blockquote>
</b> <br> <br>So to say this is a much different reading experience than the first three is an understatement, that maybe because I truly feel like I'm doing a <b>re-read</b> rather than reading new material or just because Kellan's thoughts were hard for me to pick up sometimes so I did put it down and breathe again before I delved back in. You all know the story so I'm not going to go over the plot but I will talk about/explain some of my thoughts.<br> <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/onoffgif_zps0fc03e68.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425332990ra/13878313.gif" alt=" photo onoffgif_zps0fc03e68.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>First of all this is a very lonnnnnnnggggg read and I'm not a fast reader so it took me much lonngerr time to get through it, yet when reading thoughtless I <b> Did Not Feel</b> like I was reading a big book like this, it was a rollarcoaster of a ride and I was hooked line and sinker into it, what I'm trying to put across is that I already knew what the story was about so reading a POV where there was not much change in whether it was Kellan or Kiera it dragged slightly I'm not usually one for reading the opposite pov in books but Kellan Kyle is one of My Top favourite BBF so I took a chance and I suppose S.C. Stephens voice in the male POV was weaker here. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/14251827-754F-4F36-BF02-4C8E4149233A_zps0g7cdl6o.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401733698ra/9839912.gif" alt=" photo 14251827-754F-4F36-BF02-4C8E4149233A_zps0g7cdl6o.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>First of all Keira did not come off well in Kellans head <b>AT ALL</b> I will go back to thoughtless and say that I was NOT a hater of Keira in there because I suppose I just knew who Keira was meant to be with, I just saw what happened as circumstances and because Denny was her first love I saw Keira as confused and not seeing love until it happened when Kellan entered her life so in thoughtless I did not Hate her I dealt with the emotions as they came, what I found difficult while reading Thoughtul was Kellans thought's in his head and his history how he was unable to feel love for himself how I felt like he had no self worth, he put himself last on everything and in that Keira came off as worse, she came off as not thinking about Kellen AT ALL(for me).<br> <br><b>Saying all that lets look at the positives,</b><br>I have a better understanding of Kellan with the tidbits of his past and his background being in his head meant you go through that journey right alongside him and I'm glad I learn't that bit of him yet because of that I don't think Denny should have done what he did because he knew what he went though I didn't get the thought for that, am I wrong in thinking that?? I get Denny had his heart ripped out too but I just didn't get Denny from Kellans POV what he did when reading those particular scenes I felt myself not liking Denny either. <br>Although I did enjoy the kissing and sensual moments in Thoughful Kellan melted my heart, his feelings shining through and his Intense passion and undivided attention he gave Keira when it was just them. I loved seeing why he got angry and upset and seeing a man truly deserve happiness and love it was definitely him. BUT I honestly don't think that a full length 600 page book was needed for this I really do think if it was cut in half or even a novella of particular story lines such as the rain scenes and how I finally got what was going through his head then that would of been perfect in my opinion.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/9EB191DC-F04F-4649-A9F3-845C915C99B3_zpsqknwkfpo.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425332990i/13878314._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9EB191DC-F04F-4649-A9F3-845C915C99B3_zpsqknwkfpo.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It is still 3.75 stars so it me I liked it I just didn't love it I'm so sorry, but I will say that Kellan Kyle will forever be the one Rock Star that deserves to be loved and cherished, he's the one man that I will always always love and have a special place just like Christian Grey, Kellan Kyle is exactly the same for different reasons. I'm not sure if I would recommend this but I will recommend this series its a Top Favourite of mine that I will never tire of I just didn't love his POV cause I didn't feel like I'm reading anything new and because Keira became a HATE character where I DID NOT feel like that in the rest of the series. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/D7EE59B4-F6C9-4989-949F-3AFB95D9EC4A_zpsg9dbkmdp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425332990i/13878315._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo D7EE59B4-F6C9-4989-949F-3AFB95D9EC4A_zpsg9dbkmdp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_" title="Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1331254339s/13517535.jpg" alt="Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C.   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1370050502" />
    <a title="A." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22324639-a"><img alt="A." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601824977p2/22324639.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1370050502?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A." class="user" itemprop="url" name="A." href="/user/show/22324639-a">A.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781478903130" href="/book/show/22674485-thoughtful">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=pov-hero-only">pov-hero-only</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=breaking-the-bro-code">breaking-the-bro-code</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1370050502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10766684345764429227"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423915791ra/13689178.gif' width='400"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was my very first audiobook and let me tell you, it’s not as easy as it sounds and the experience is certainly different. Sure, listening to an audiobook is very practical, but if you’re more visually oriented person like me, it takes some time to adjust. I didn’t know what to do with my hands and my eyes at first, however stupid that sounds. Another problem was that sometimes I couldn’t focus, my thoughts often wandered off somewhere or the narrator’s voice lulled to sleep. But on</span>
  <span id="freeText10766684345764429227" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423915791ra/13689178.gif" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was my very first audiobook and let me tell you, it’s not as easy as it sounds and the experience is certainly different. Sure, listening to an audiobook is very practical, but if you’re more visually oriented person like me, it takes some time to adjust. I didn’t know what to do with my hands and my eyes at first, however stupid that sounds. Another problem was that sometimes I couldn’t focus, my thoughts often wandered off somewhere or the narrator’s voice lulled to sleep. But once I got used to it, I was one hundred percent invested in the story.<br><br>As for the story, I loved the first three books and it was really nice to relive all the events through Kellan’s eyes. However, I already knew pretty much everything that would happen so this book wasn’t angsty enough for my liking nor did it keep me on the edge of my seat like the first three books did. <br><br>I also struggled with the inner monologue at times, I felt like there was too much telling and not enough showing. Thankfully, the male narrator was very good otherwise I would have been bored as hell.<br><br>A lot of readers complained that Kellan’s point of view was too “feminine” but I don’t agree. Kellan is not an über alpha, he’s a more laid-back kind of guy. He's a very sexual and sensual person so I think his voice in this book was just fine.<br><br>Despite some minor issues, I still enjoyed this book. And Kellan consolidated his place as one of the sexiest and hottest book boyfriends in the romance genre.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470076569ra/19886047.gif" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>QUICK REVIEW:</b><br><br><b>Enjoyment:</b>: 3.5/5<br><b>Writing style:</b> 4/5<br><b>Storyline:</b> 3/5<br><b>Hero:</b> 5/5<br><b>Heroine:</b> 3/5<br><b>Secondary characters:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Hotness/chemistry:</b> 5/5 <br><b>Romance:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Angst:</b> 3/5<br><b>Darkness level:</b> 2/5<br><b>Humor:</b> 3/5<br><b> Depth of the book:</b> 4/5<br><b>POV:</b> hero, 1st person<br><b> Triggers:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[cheating, love triangle, child abuse <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1082131677" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082131677" />
    <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady"><img alt="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370640721p2/14351108.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1082131677?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=family-series-romance-sexy">family-series-romance-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=rock-movie-star">rock-movie-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1082131677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2259039559516612162"><b>3 "I'm Sorry" Stars</b><br/><br/>I can't tell you how happy I was when I heard that this book was going to be written. I Loved The Thoughtless Series and I loved Kellan and Kiera. Thoughtless was a tough book because of the cheating content but the growth of the characters through the entire series was spectacular. While there are many Kiera haters, I was not one of them, she was young and in a situation that was hard to navigate but in the end, all was wonderful.<br/><br/><b>So back to Thoughtful</b>......this is Kellan Kyle</span>
  <span id="freeText2259039559516612162" style="display:none"><b>3 "I'm Sorry" Stars</b><br><br>I can't tell you how happy I was when I heard that this book was going to be written. I Loved The Thoughtless Series and I loved Kellan and Kiera. Thoughtless was a tough book because of the cheating content but the growth of the characters through the entire series was spectacular. While there are many Kiera haters, I was not one of them, she was young and in a situation that was hard to navigate but in the end, all was wonderful.<br><br><b>So back to Thoughtful</b>......this is Kellan Kyle's thoughts in Thoughtless. As Thoughtless was written from Kiera's POV, we never got see what Kellan was thinking. So I go super lucky and got an ARC from NG and I was over the moon. So I jumped in all excited......<br><br>This book was not easy. It was sad, heartbreaking, gut-wrenching, depressing, angsty, and it was just hard to read. As I knew the ending, that was the only thing that kept me going. I loved Kellan before, and while reading, my heart expanded for him, it ached for him and if I could, I would have jumped into the story to hug him and let him know that he was not alone. Kellan's childhood was not rosy and happy, it was unloving and painful. It hurt me to read and see how he <b>Thought</b> of himself. He never knew love so how would anyone really ever love him, choose him? <br><br>What I truly loved was at 6%..... Kellan's reaction to Kiera. I am one of those people who believe that people can know when they meet that one person that completes them. Does it always work, no, but I do believe that it exists and I believe that Kellan was 100% convinced that his life would be forever changed by the girl that walked in the door at Pete's that one faithful night. I absolutely loved reading that he knew.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/ee727ee3849cf6c2ca0f1208b84c00c3_zpsum9j9vkc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424143286i/13721158.jpg" alt=" photo ee727ee3849cf6c2ca0f1208b84c00c3_zpsum9j9vkc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So as you know, the rest of the story is one of struggle. Kiera was in the middle of 2 men that love her and that she loved back. This book follows Thoughtless exactly. I will be very honest....I think that this book should have been a novella. I would have loved reading just the pivotal scenes in his thoughts. I found this book to be too long and too heartbreaking. I knew the ending and it should have sustained me but reading and feeling sad for most of the book was overwhelming. Hearing his past, hearing his wants, needs and desires for Kiera just got too much in my opinion. Kiera got blamed for a lot in her book, but Kellan was just as responsible. Their communication was always sweet and suggestive, they never really expressed their true feelings, they assumed things, they were mean and vindictive to one another, and they were young, inexperienced and made mistakes. Their trials and tribulations were heightened because this was a triangle, feelings had to be hurt and someone would lose in the end. <br><br>I'm very mixed in recommending this book. I really loved parts of it but I struggled with a lot of it. I pushed myself to finish and that isn't a feeling that I wanted. I am sure I am in the minority but I do want you to know that I Adore Kellan and Kiera and The Entire Thoughtless Series. This book just did me in and I would have liked less.<br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by Grand Central Publishing in exchange for an honest review.</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2259039559516612162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
