<div id="review_819844810" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/819844810" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/819844810?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer819844810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10933784020868945226"><br/>Since this is essentially the same story as <i>Thoughtless</i> but from Kellan's POV, I won't be doing a regular review on the story. I'll just be posting my views on our all time favorite rocker! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425063159ra/13839231.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>(Love that little smirk!)</i><br/><br/>I knew this book would be <b>difficult</b> but I really had no idea how bad it would be! At moments I wanted to hug Kellan and at the same time be the <i>fourth</i> person to smack his face!<br/><br/>Kellan just feels so deeply and I think it's because he's shut down his feelings for so long. When he starts </span>
  <span id="freeText10933784020868945226" style="display:none"><br>Since this is essentially the same story as <i>Thoughtless</i> but from Kellan's POV, I won't be doing a regular review on the story. I'll just be posting my views on our all time favorite rocker! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425063159ra/13839231.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(Love that little smirk!)</i><br><br>I knew this book would be <b>difficult</b> but I really had no idea how bad it would be! At moments I wanted to hug Kellan and at the same time be the <i>fourth</i> person to smack his face!<br><br>Kellan just feels so deeply and I think it's because he's shut down his feelings for so long. When he starts connecting with Kiera, he can hardly believe it and he opens himself up. The range of his emotions in this book was exhausting but...he was able to get a handle on things.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425063159ra/13839232.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*Warning* if you weren't a big fan of Kiera's in <i>Thoughtless</i>, you will probably be even less of a fan in this one. I didn't have a problem with her in <i>Thoughtless</i> especially since we had her POV and we knew what she was going through. Not getting her POV and hearing the things she says to Kellan was rough. The saving grace was knowing the outcome. <br><br>And the intensity is certainly present in the steamy scenes! Just getting to read those from Kellan's POV made everything worth it! ;) <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412744074ra/11416472.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because this book is l-o-n-g...just like all the others but tough + long + exhausting is a little hard to put up with. It really picked up after the fifty percent mark...thank goodness because I almost "pinched my nose" to stop from getting a headache! <br><br>One of my favorite things was getting more story on Kellan's relationships with the other band members especially Evan. I loved how they played off each other and how they worked together on their music. <br><br>Of course, everything works out in the end. My favorite book is <i>Effortless</i> and I would love to read it from his POV but I doubt that will happen. <br><br>Griffin's book, <i>Untamed</i>, is next...coming out November 5, 2015. Naturally, it looks like Griffin's gonna cause all kinds of drama! <br><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787081i/491245.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "Girlfriend. I'd never had one before." <br><br>♥ “Well…you’re just more talented with your fingers,” she replied.<br><br>♥ “Jesus. Think we ought to get him an ice pack?”<br><br>♥ "Because you're mine!" <br><br>♥ “You do realize that if you keep doing this to my body, I will never be able to have children?”<br><br>♥ "Your real parents may have been shit, but the three of us, we’re your family now. Get that through your damn skull!”<br><br>♥ “You’re…the only woman I’ve ever loved…ever."<br><br>♥ “I’m with you…I’m right here.”<br><br><br>♦ BR w/Melissa &amp; Patty!<br><br><br><br><i>(Prior to Review)</i><br><br>If these deleted scenes are any indication, this is gonna be a hard book to read!! Poor Kellan! :(<br><br>♦ Deleted scene 1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://authorscstephens.com/thoughtful-deleted-scene-1/">http://authorscstephens.com/thoughtfu...</a><br><br>♦ Deleted scene 2: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://authorscstephens.com/thoughtful-deleted-scene-2/">http://authorscstephens.com/thoughtfu...</a><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>*update 7/22/14 - She signed w/Forever books so Kellan's book will be released February 2015, Griffin's book Fall 2015 and a new book - Spring 2016!! </b><br><br><br><br><br><i>3/11 Teaser:<br><br><br>She handed me the necklace, and my fingers were shaking as I took it. The guitar was perfectly crafted, delicate, but sturdy, and there was a large circle diamond in the center that sparkled in the lights. It was me, and it was Kiera…the perfect embodiment of what we were, or rather, what we’d never be. I couldn’t think of anything better to give her, to help her remember me, and what we’d gone through. “I’ll take it,” I whispered, not even looking at the price tag.<br><br>“Excellent,” the woman beamed. “I’ll go ring you up.”<br><br>While she walked away, Evan stepped up to me. “Kellan…you can’t expect her to wear that. It’s too obvious.”<br><br>I shook my head as I stared at the glow emanating from the diamond. “I don’t expect her to. I don’t expect anything. But this is what I want to give her.” My eyes were watering when I looked over at him. “This is how I want to say goodbye.”</i><br><br><br><br><b>1/14 Teaser: <br><br>"When the coffee was done, I prepared our cups, and set Kiera's down in front of her. I leaned back in my chair, perfectly content as I drank mine. Kiera hunched over her mug like she was freezing and it was the only source of warmth in the room. I knew her reaction wasn’t from the cold though, and knowing that made my smile even wider. Jealousy is a bitch, isn’t it, Kiera?"<br><br>Cannot Wait!!</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650953.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_961974332" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/961974332" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/961974332?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=motha-whiplash-emotions">motha-whiplash-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=arc-reads">arc-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=fluffy-fluffer">fluffy-fluffer</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=imma-hit-that-bitch">imma-hit-that-bitch</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=killing-me-with-sexual-tension">killing-me-with-sexual-tension</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer961974332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5743754719482595750"><b>3 STARS! ★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424334612i/13748306.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"For a minute, I could pretend that I meant everything to her, because she was certainly starting to mean everything to me."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Y'all know I'm a self-proclaimed angst-whore but if there's any book I've read that managed to cause a massive explosion of blood vessels and induce Kindle-throwing outburst, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_' title='Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens' rel='nofollow noopener'>Thoughtless</a> is <i>THE ONE.</i> Everytime I think about that book and the most indecisive heroine that is Keira, the amount of RAGE I feel is enough to cause me stomach ulcers. But alas there's</span>
  <span id="freeText5743754719482595750" style="display:none"><b>3 STARS! ★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424334612i/13748306.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"For a minute, I could pretend that I meant everything to her, because she was certainly starting to mean everything to me."</i>
</b><br><br>Y'all know I'm a self-proclaimed angst-whore but if there's any book I've read that managed to cause a massive explosion of blood vessels and induce Kindle-throwing outburst, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_" title="Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens" rel="nofollow noopener">Thoughtless</a> is <i>THE ONE.</i> Everytime I think about that book and the most indecisive heroine that is Keira, the amount of RAGE I feel is enough to cause me stomach ulcers. But alas there's Kellan Kyle that completely redeemed the initial read for me and being one of my all-time favorite book boyfriends, I couldn't pass on the chance to be inside his head this time around.<br><br>Let me first reiterate the obvious: <b>This is purely a retelling of Thoughtless.</b> It's literally Thoughtless: Kellan's POV, so if you're going in hoping for fresh material, you might be disappointed. Being in Kellan's head brings you on an emotional journey as you get to live through the angst and heartbreak again and most importantly, the extra bit that wasn't present in the first one which lets us delve into his childhood past that left him those emotional scars. <br><br>I really appreciated those parts the most as it gave me the closure I needed to understand what made him so broken on the inside, being drowned in that sea of loneliness and how he came to found solace in Keira. My heart really hurt for him with those scenes and once again brought up those ragey feels in me that had me yelling that Keira didn't deserve him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424337953i/13748835.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>However I found it off-putting that Kellan's POV wasn't what I expected at all. For a good portion of the read, his inner monologue came off as clingy &amp; borderline obsessive for Keira, it was like a truckload of repetitiveness of how much he loved her and couldn't let her go. I could feel myself cringing at his choice of words and his train of thoughts that could have easily passed off as a girl's POV. Also, a lot of scenes dragged on more than I like which nearly sent me into a snoozefest and I couldn't find it in myself to be fully immersed in this lengthy read. Perhaps I would have preferred it better if it leaned towards a novella read instead of a full-length novel. But that's just my opinion :)<br><br>Overall, <u>Thoughtful</u> wasn't as angsty as I hoped to be especially since I'm already well aware to anticipate the trainwreck that awaited me. Although with the minor issues in this read, I'm still glad that we finally got to read Kellan's side of the story and appreciate getting to understand what shaped him to be that rockstar we all came to love. Honestly had this been any other read, I'd rate it less but Kellan Kyle holds such a dear place in my heart since the very beginning and reading this surely stirred back up those strong emotions in me ♥ <br><br>I think it's safe to say that fans of Kellan Kyle who have been dying to get any bits of him since the end of the trilogy will rejoice in getting their Kellan fix. But be prepared to have your heart break all over again for him just like in Thoughtless. <br> <br><i>ARC kindly provided by Forever (Grand Central Publishing) via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5743754719482595750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14911260407696974605"><b>*** 3,5 stars ***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298599ra/685795.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm glad I had this book on audio because if I were to read it, I would have probably DNFed. I am so mad I gave this one a go, I wish I hadn't and could still remember the story the way it was when reading Thoughtless. <br/><br/>It wasn't bad but I somehow didn't enjoy it. Kellan turned out to be too whiny, Kiera was her indecisive mean-self (hurting one and stringing the other along) and I only felt sorry for Danny. Sorry. <br>Well, I will just keep picturing Kellan in my head looking like this and hopefully I will forget about his inner emotional turmoil, which was a bit too overdone for me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448364914i/17130125.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_822405205" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/822405205" />
    <a title="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog"><img alt="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514480818p2/3243151.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/822405205?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " href="/user/show/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog">✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=all-time-favorite-series">all-time-favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=arc-provided-by-author-or-publisher">arc-provided-by-author-or-publisher</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=must-read-author">must-read-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=five-big-and-fat-stars">five-big-and-fat-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=i-loved-it">i-loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=must-have-tissues">must-have-tissues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=keeper">keeper</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=bookboyfriend-number-one">bookboyfriend-number-one</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog?shelf=first-reads">first-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer822405205" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15510499784104532878"><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423909436i/13688814._SY540_.jpg' width='380' height='380' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423909436i/13688815._SX540_.jpg' width='389' height='188' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Do we all remember what happened in #Thoughtless? When Kiera told us her story??<br/><br/>Now it's Kellan's turn. And I just know that it's going to be sooo amazing. And so sad and moving and frustrating and just beautiful.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389637658ra/8044946.gif' width='360' height='241' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To prepare for #Thoughtful, I re-read the whole series. I just couldn't help myself. Kellan is my all-time-favorite Book Boyfriend!! ♥ But now I'm not so sure if the re-reading was wrong - it might've been better to go at THOUGHTFUL with a bit distance to the whole story - it's not li</span>
  <span id="freeText15510499784104532878" style="display:none"><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423909436i/13688814._SY540_.jpg" width="380" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423909436i/13688815._SX540_.jpg" width="389" height="188" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do we all remember what happened in #Thoughtless? When Kiera told us her story??<br><br>Now it's Kellan's turn. And I just know that it's going to be sooo amazing. And so sad and moving and frustrating and just beautiful.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389637658ra/8044946.gif" width="360" height="241" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To prepare for #Thoughtful, I re-read the whole series. I just couldn't help myself. Kellan is my all-time-favorite Book Boyfriend!! ♥ But now I'm not so sure if the re-reading was wrong - it might've been better to go at THOUGHTFUL with a bit distance to the whole story - it's not like I ever forgot anything that happened anyway ☺<br><br>If you haven't read the Thoughtless series yet...<br><br><b>
  <u>PLEASE STOP READING THE REVIEW NOW!!!!</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422040127ra/13448487.gif" width="320" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>THOUGHTFUL starts a few weeks before Kiera &amp; Denny arrive in Seattle.<br><br>We see a bit about how Kellan goes about his 'rockstar' life. All his random hook-ups. He loves sex, sure, but it's so much more than that. He just wants to be close to someone. Even if it's just for a few minutes or hours. He loves being touched, because he never had any of that growing up. He desperately wants to connect to someone. He's not yet really sure what exactly it is that he wants (like a real loving relationship for example) - he just knows that it feels amazing to chase away the lonliness for a short while.<br><br>He's sooo excited once he knows Denny will move in with him. That's so adorable to read.<br><br>Denny is the only person - other than his band-members - that he ever loved.<br><br>He sees Denny as his only real family.<br><br>He can't wait to re-connect with him.<br><br>But unfortunately he is immediately attracted to Kiera. Like - amazingly drawn to her.<br><br>The first second he sees her at Pete's - he's almost a changed person. And that's when he thought he might have a chance at her, because he hadn't yet seen that she came in with Denny ...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>but this girl ... even seeing her through a crowd, there was something about her that sang to me. It nearly stopped me in my tracks.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>As you can imagine - all through the book we suffer with Kellan. Ok, not only Kellan - we love Denny too and we know how the story ends, and Denny will not get the girl in the end.<br><br>But this is Kellan's story and he just, ugh - I could've cried all through the book. He's just so lonely, especially in the beginning. He just wants someone to love him. To have a girl look at him the way Kiera looks at Denny. He's so amazed by their relationship - he's never witnessed anything like that before.<br><br>Then of course they become closer - especially once Denny is gone for those two months.<br><br>And even though Kellan knows he has to stay away from her - to stop thinking and dreaming inappropriate things about her - he just can't.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423909436i/13688816.jpg" width="361" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>OK - THAT'S ALL I'M TELLING YOU!!! ☺<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380223307ra/681040.gif" width="250" height="216" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>____________________________________<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399919844i/9609886.png" width="390" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One word:<br>A.M.A.Z.I.N.G.</b><br><br>I'm the first one to say that I usually don't much like it when an author writes the same story from a different POV much later. But this one was just so different.<br><br>First of all - Kellan is my all time favorite guy. Plus, we know there are soo many moments in Thoughtless where Kellan is gone and we only have Kiera's story.<br><br>We also finally want to know what Kellan thinks, how he feels, what he thinks and wishes and hopes.<br><br>All those moments we never got to hear in Kiera's version.... like the first time he saw her... what he felt and thought about falling for his 'brother's' girl.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>She was awkward, shy, adorable, and beautiful.<br>A deadly combination.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>This book was just sooooo full of emotion.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423909436i/13688817._SY540_.jpg" width="380" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Being with her meant everything to me.<br>She meant everything to me.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422040131ra/13448490.gif" width="245" height="137" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Like I said before - Dawson and I - we had lots of tears in our eyes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435459ra/879762.gif" width="380" height="179" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't want to pity this amazing rockstar (he wouldn't want that☺) - but you can't help but see this small sad boy with his guitar. How he started sleeping with women, just to feel a tiny little bit of affection in his love-less life.<br><br>Then at the end - I will not spoil it - but there's this adorable fact about Kellan's everyday coffee-meeting greeting to Kiera, that we never knew... but now he finally tells us. I loved it.<br><br><br><b>I loved every second of Kellan's story.<br><br><i>THOUGHTFUL was an amazingly beautiful &amp; emotional addition to the Thoughtless series. If you loved Kellan Kyle before, you will be even more in love with him now!</i><br><br>FIVE BIG AND FAT STARS!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398584987i/9437605.png" width="385" height="149" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now please Hollywood, make Kellan into a TV or Movie-star - ASAP!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/563406.gif" width="380" height="177" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>PLEASE!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442943030i/16296666.png" width="370" height="58" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://amzn.to/1vEQvEw" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412783863i/11422441.png" width="138" height="37" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://amzn.to/1rP4SWn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412783863i/11422442.png" width="138" height="37" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://amzn.to/1BH6Kmw" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412783863i/11422443.png" width="138" height="37" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1166376052" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1166376052" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1166376052?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1166376052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17652447852585956054"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421366246i/13367072._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5++ EMOTIONAL STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><b> ‘I would never be the same after this. We would never be the same after this.’</b><br/><br/>We’ll start by saying if you haven’t already done so; we strongly suggest reading Thoughtless <b>before</b> reading this book. Although set in the same timeframe, reading Thoughtful will allow you to experience the shift in this story told from Kellan’s perspective. And secondly……Arrrrggghhh this book! <b>Our hearts!</b> We are exhausted! Emotionally wrung out!<br/><br/><b>‘I wrapped my fury around me like armor. Let her t</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17652447852585956054" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421366246i/13367072._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5++ EMOTIONAL STARS!!!</b><br><br><b> ‘I would never be the same after this. We would never be the same after this.’</b><br><br>We’ll start by saying if you haven’t already done so; we strongly suggest reading Thoughtless <b>before</b> reading this book. Although set in the same timeframe, reading Thoughtful will allow you to experience the shift in this story told from Kellan’s perspective. And secondly……Arrrrggghhh this book! <b>Our hearts!</b> We are exhausted! Emotionally wrung out!<br><br><b>‘I wrapped my fury around me like armor. Let her try to find a crack. I dared her.’</b><br><br>We’ll be honest. We were a bit nervous when we heard Thoughtful was in the works. Kellan was, and still is, one of our <b>favourite book boyfriends</b> with the Thoughtless series being forever embedded in our hearts. It goes without saying too much of Kellan is never enough, but still, we had concerns.<br><br>Firstly, we knew Kellan’s story would be painful. We <b>felt his pain, loneliness and confusion</b> enough in Thoughtless, hearing it from Kellan first hand was definitely going to be difficult and would add a new dimension to Thoughtless that we weren’t sure we were prepared for.<br><br><b>‘Being in love was so hard. But not being in love was even worse.’</b><br><br>Another concern was this being the same book from a different perspective. It’s been done before and in some cases it’s worked brilliantly by enhancing the original story, yet in others it’s damaged the original story beyond repair. We know SC Stephens is a brilliant storyteller who evokes strong emotions in her words and that she fervently loves her characters, but nonetheless there was a part of us that worried this book could fall in the latter and that would have broken our hearts.<br><br><b>‘It was so hard to see her in pain. It was even harder to know I was the source of it. I was tormenting her, she said so herself.’</b><br><br>But we<b> HAD</b> to delve in and we’re thrilled to say Thoughtful definitely fell into the former, as <b>Kellan’s POV positively enhanced</b> what was already one of our all-time favourite books. It felt fresh, new and gave us insights that had us aching, smiling and <b>falling love with Kellan</b> and this book all over again! <br><br><b>‘I was not about to give her the satisfaction of seeing my pain. My emotional pain anyway. That was mine, she didn’t have a right to it.’</b><br><br>Told from Kellan’s perspective his words were heartbreaking, passionate and highly emotional. Kellan wears his heart on his sleeve and we felt, lived and breathed everything Kellan went through. The depth of his anger, frustration, confusion and love, his unexpected feelings for Kiera, <b>WE! FELT! EVERYTHING!</b> Deep in our hearts.<br><br><b>‘I knew, without a doubt in my head, that I could fall asleep with her in my arms every night and be completely happy. And that thought, scared the crap out of me, because on the flip side, I knew I would be completely miserable without her.’</b><br><br>There’s no doubting this relationship was toxic not only to themselves but those around them and through Kellan’s eyes we really experienced that aspect of the story.<br><br><b>‘The three of us all living together could be an incredible, eye-opening experience. Or it could be a living nightmare. Either way, it was definitely going to be interesting.’</b><br><br>We’ve been asked by readers if this book is merely a rehash?” Our answer is <b>NO</b>, it most certainly didn’t feel that way to us at all. Sure, parts of dialogue are carried through from Thoughtless but they are brought about in a new light making them feel very new and different in Thoughtful. SC Stephens has also explored and expanded scenes and delved into the dynamics of Kellan’s other relationships besides his and Kiera’s making Thoughtful such an enlightening experience.<br><br>The relationships with Kellan and Denny, and Kellan and the band were fleshed out in Thoughtful, and in particular Kellan’s relationship with Evan was something we really enjoyed. We knew these two had a bond, but the depth of that bond was so heart-warming.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t let her go, Evan. I tried. I tried to stay away, I tried to forget her.”</i>
</b><br><br>The relationship between Denny and Kellan is also one which SC Stephens took to another level in Thoughtful. This time around we really felt the brotherhood between these two men, making the utter betrayal and hurt Kiera and Kellan caused Denny all the more painful to experience.<br><br><b>‘I’d wanted her, so I’d taken her. I was no friend to him, to anyone. ‘</b><br><br>Although we all knew the outcome, the journey to the final destination in Thoughtful felt new and different allowing us to really feel what was going through Kellan’s head throughout this tumultuous and passionate relationship.<br><br><b>‘If she was going to be a bitch, then I would be her bastard.’</b><br><br>We’ve no doubt fans of this series are going to <b>love this book.</b> It really does offer up a new level to the original story and through it all we felt the gut wrenching <b>agony,</b> the <b>anger</b>, the <b>hurt</b>, the joy, the loss, the <b>passion and the absolute love</b> experienced by this man upon finding his soulmate. <b>**WARNING: Have tissues at the ready!!</b> You’ll need them…we did!!! Prepare to let Kellan Kyle steal your heart all over again. Oh Kellan….sigh….you have our hearts buddy!<br><br><i>**Reviewed from an ARC copy provided by Grand Central Publishing, with thanks.’<br>***Please note: Quotes may/may not be included in final release***</i><br><br><a href="http://wp.me/p2WbFf-37" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review of Thoughtless - Book One</a><br><a href="http://wp.me/p2WbFf-2r" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review of Effortless- Book Two </a><br><a href="http://wp.me/p2WbFf-1y8" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review of Reckless Book Three</a><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✦✦&lt; TB Blog :<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦✦✦ Come say Hi : <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦✦✦Follow us: <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦✦✦Check out: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a> <br>✦✦✦ We're on TSU: <a href="https://www.tsu.co/TBBLOG" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on TSU</a></span>

<div id="review_823375581" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/823375581" />
    <a title="Kelli C " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c"><img alt="Kelli C " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426900480p2/14931216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823375581?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli C " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli C " href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c">Kelli C </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=fab-writing">fab-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=hot-rock-stars">hot-rock-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=must-reads">must-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=steamy-read">steamy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=taboo-love">taboo-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823375581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13424838145182004821">I am not afraid to admit that the <i>Thoughtless Series</i> is my "go to" read when I'm in a funk! There is no better, for me, than Kellen Kyle when it comes to book BF's. He was my first literary crush and to have 300 some pages of his most inner thoughts and feelings just staggered me.<br/><br/>Reading <i>Thoughtful</i> brought back so many of my favorite scenes...coffee and stolen cuddles with a moody rock God, passion ignited in an empty expresso stand, and the love-hate combustion of emotions in the rain. I was ag</span>
  <span id="freeText13424838145182004821" style="display:none">I am not afraid to admit that the <i>Thoughtless Series</i> is my "go to" read when I'm in a funk! There is no better, for me, than Kellen Kyle when it comes to book BF's. He was my first literary crush and to have 300 some pages of his most inner thoughts and feelings just staggered me.<br><br>Reading <i>Thoughtful</i> brought back so many of my favorite scenes...coffee and stolen cuddles with a moody rock God, passion ignited in an empty expresso stand, and the love-hate combustion of emotions in the rain. I was again on edge and I was again completely affected. But with the good comes the bad, and that was the re-acquaintance of Kiera Allen. While I admit to not being a fan of hers, seeing her thru Kellen's eyes and heart was twice as devastating.<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1424435153393_zpsh4k53lwv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424455839i/13763964.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1424435153393_zpsh4k53lwv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I won't rehash the whole sordid tale of Kellen and Kiera, instead I will just say that I had no idea the depth of Kellen's soul. He was truly a broken man who wanted nothing more than for someone to "stay," to let him know he was worth something. He wanted...no he NEEDED to be loved. While many can't stomach the fact that his heart wanted Kiera, you cannot read the inner workings of Kellen and completely not"get it."<br><br><b>"...the way she listened to my music, the way she looked at me with so much compassion. Like she understood my pain even if she didn't know what it was...Why did I have to care about her?...Why couldn't she just love me the way I loved her."</b> <br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1424435848724_zpsffkjtlc9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424455839i/13763965.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1424435848724_zpsffkjtlc9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"I hated her so much. Only I didn't. I don't hate her at all, I didn't even blame her. I wouldn't want me either."</b><br><br>Heartbreaking. Sexy. Insightful. For those who cringe at triangles and abhor cheating, take a read into the mind of a man who fell in love so hard and struggled everyday with his worth. The highs and lows of acceptance, the passion and the pain of pleasure are palpable. Kellen's journey to Kiera was not pretty and it was quite selfish and life damming, yet it was all consuming.<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/0432dbb2-39cc-4ada-9bb7-deaa1fd6a72e_zps769535ee.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424455840i/13763966.jpg" alt=" photo 0432dbb2-39cc-4ada-9bb7-deaa1fd6a72e_zps769535ee.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In the end, I came away even more of a fan then I ever thought possible. While yes, I had to endure the insecurities and complete bullshit of Kiera, it could not ruin my high from falling in love all over again with a broken man and his epic love story. If Kiera was the balm to Kellen's pain then thank you S.C. Stephens for letting me understand why!!!<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1424435664045_zpsfv0zplgx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424455840i/13763967._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1424435664045_zpsfv0zplgx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>*ARC graciously provided per publisher via NetGalley in exchange for honest review*</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13424838145182004821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10973212153425727937">★★★★ <b>3.5 Stars</b> ★★★★<br/><br/><b>Now LIVE!<br/>Amazon - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1ApIw35'>http://amzn.to/1ApIw35</a><br/>Amazon UK - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1ENgpuw'>http://amzn.to/1ENgpuw</a></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424026740i/13705428.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Thoughtful</i> is the highly anticipated novel that gives us <i>Thoughtless</i> in Kellan's Point of View. Thoughtless is one of my <b>favourite angsty books of all time</b> so even though I normally avoid the retelling of books like the plague, I really wanted to be able to feel Kellan's pain through his own eyes.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424026740i/13705427._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The book starts a few weeks before he meets Keira and we are reacquainted with Pete's Bar, The D-Bags and all</span>
  <span id="freeText10973212153425727937" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>3.5 Stars</b> ★★★★<br><br><b>Now LIVE!<br>Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1ApIw35">http://amzn.to/1ApIw35</a><br>Amazon UK - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1ENgpuw">http://amzn.to/1ENgpuw</a></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424026740i/13705428.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Thoughtful</i> is the highly anticipated novel that gives us <i>Thoughtless</i> in Kellan's Point of View. Thoughtless is one of my <b>favourite angsty books of all time</b> so even though I normally avoid the retelling of books like the plague, I really wanted to be able to feel Kellan's pain through his own eyes.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424026740i/13705427._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book starts a few weeks before he meets Keira and we are reacquainted with Pete's Bar, The D-Bags and all the people that we grew to love in the Thoughtless trilogy. This is where we begin to feel the <b>loneliness</b> that Kellan has been experiencing all his life, with snippets from his past with his parents and the reasons that he feels the need to bed any attractive woman that shows an interest. Kellan just want's to feel an emotional connection and be loved.<br><br>When Denny and Keira move into Kellan's house we watch him fall more and more in love with the girl that he can't have without betraying his best friend.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424026740i/13705426._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>_ _ _ _<br><br>There were some great moments, my heart broke for Kellan all over again as Keira constantly chooses Denny over him and I really came to understand his motives for treating Keira the was he did when she hurt him and Keira made me feel just as annoyed at her as I did the first time round.<br><br>My reason for not rating this book higher was the length, I felt that it dragged in parts, probably because I have read it all before but Kellan seemed to have <b>very detailed thoughts</b> that really could have been condensed down a bit. I found myself skimming certain scenes in order to get to the juicy bits.<br><br>If you are a Kellan fan, it's definitely worth a read just to get inside his head and spend some more time with one of the <b>best Rockstar book boyfriends of all time.</b><br><br>Whilst this can be technically read as a standalone, I would recommend reading Thoughtless first for the full angst effect.<br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from Little, Brown Book Group UK in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://ilovebooklove-ab.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_824290219" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/824290219" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/824290219?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=arc-netgalley">arc-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=not-released-yet">not-released-yet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=skim-tastic">skim-tastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=my-favorite-covers">my-favorite-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=it-aint-easy-bein-cheesy">it-aint-easy-bein-cheesy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer824290219" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15676894012700015974"><b>*2.5 stars*</b> <br/><br/>**I'd like to put a disclaimer before I even start this review: S.C. Stephens is an amazing author and she is one of my favorites. Nothing I say below has changed my opinion of her as an author....I just wanted so much more because I know how awesome she can be.**<br/><br/><b>Did she realize I screamed my heart out in my lyrics? Did she understand that my life left me feeling vacant inside? That I was so fucking lonely I almost couldn't stand myself?</b> << Love this line.<br/><br/>This hurts me to say, worse </span>
  <span id="freeText15676894012700015974" style="display:none"><b>*2.5 stars*</b> <br><br>**I'd like to put a disclaimer before I even start this review: S.C. Stephens is an amazing author and she is one of my favorites. Nothing I say below has changed my opinion of her as an author....I just wanted so much more because I know how awesome she can be.**<br><br><b>Did she realize I screamed my heart out in my lyrics? Did she understand that my life left me feeling vacant inside? That I was so fucking lonely I almost couldn't stand myself?</b> &lt;&lt; Love this line.<br><br>This hurts me to say, worse than any of you can imagine but....this book was <i>so unnecessary.</i> It's exactly what I thought. I shouldn't have read it and, in the end, it took some of the magic away from book one of the series. I can't help it, though. I needed this book. BAD. And here I am, disappointed. But what right do I have? I requested it and was just positive I would get denied. I played Russian Roulette and found myself on the receiving end of the bullet. But, even more than that-<b>I wanted this book to be glorious.</b> I wanted to experience all the same emotions as I did with <i>Thoughtless, Effortless, Reckless</i>....it's not possible. Not for me, anyway.<br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_n9lpj8kKAM1tiv932o1_500_zpsdyei9ndr.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423074042ra/13584643.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n9lpj8kKAM1tiv932o1_500_zpsdyei9ndr.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kellan Kyle is one of my absolute favorite book boyfriends. It's something anyone close to me is more than aware of-<b>I adore this guy.</b> Thank God, though, my opinion of him hasn't changed like it did with Travis from the massacre <i>Walking Disaster.</i> Some things should just be left sacred. I'm sorry, but some books and series should be <b>left the fuck alone.</b> This is one of them. <br><br>That's not to say I didn't enjoy certain parts. I'll admit it-I'll admit that! I could NEVER HATE my favorite scenes in the history of holy hotness-<i>The lime scene, the coffee stand scene, the dance club scene, the RAIN SCENE for fuck's sake!!!</i> But I just...I don't get it. Why did he fall for Kiera in this book? How? And it makes no sense because we're in his head and he's sitting here telling us why he loves her, but as with ALL male POV re-dos...Kiera just wasn't Kiera. And oh, here we go, I hear all the boo-hisses from all those who loathed her, but guess what? I liked her. She fucked up-Royally. She really did. And, yes, she really annoyed me when I read <i>Thoughtless</i> two years ago. But, the fact remains, I still <i>liked her.</i> I did. She made a mistake-no, she made mistake after costly mistake. But Lord, I've said it before and I'll say it again-I can barely even choose where to eat lunch!! How in the ever loving fuck am I supposed to choose between two hot, supportive, amazing guys? That's the question, though, isn't it? You shouldn't get yourself into that position, anyway. But, would I be able to hold up under that pressure after I thought my forever-love had abandoned me for his career?? I. Don't. Know. I'd like to think so, but I've never been, or put myself, in that position. I don't condone cheating at any cost, but this is fiction, people! And I'm circling my point-<b>I didn't feel even a fraction of the angst, emotion, or heartache that I did with it's namesake.</b> I didn't. When authors switch sides, we lose all that depth and all that hard work that was put into the main female character. We know her now, sure, because we read that book. But guess what-This book is not the same book. I want to see it all again. I want to see him fall in love with a real person, not a stand-in or a mannequin of the girl we are supposed to know. This Kiera, she wasn't a betrayer or an adulterer or even a confused young girl anymore...she was, simply put, just another piece of paper. That girl that I was angry at and cried for was not here. I know people wanted more Kellan and that was the whole point, but....is he supposed to be the <i>only</i> character?<br><br><b>I'd seen anger, jealousy, bitterness, and resentment. Love equaled pain in my world. And I generally tried to avoid pain.</b><br><br>It's so hard to explain and people most likely won't get it, but I need two complex characters. Two characters that make me rip my hair out and who fight each other and who LOVE PASSIONATELY even as they live in sin. I love Kellan so much, more than anyone could know....but this story didn't do him justice. I liked a little mystery to his character. I liked his smokey looks and secret glances her way. Being told he's doing such things takes all the breathtaking imagery away and hands me a formulaic script for what I already know: Kellan loves Kiera. God, don't I know it. But I wanted to see them fall in love all over again-from his eyes. And if you take all the mystery, the angst, the 'I don't know what's going to happen', and the heated conversations, you stunt what was already an amazing (albeit controversial) book. Tell me....what do you have left?<br><br>With less inner dialogue it would have changed the story, in a good way. Hearing a play by play of every little conversation is where it all went downhill. Telling instead of showing and hearing instead of seeing really halted the flow. A lot of times we were left hanging and days would pass. That's fine, sure, but don't say 'over the last three days, Kiera started to give me evil looks-I needed to talk to her about that.' That's not an actual line, but it gives you the gist. I just didn't care for this and I never have in any story. <br><br><b>I'd never experienced anything like this before. It was beyond all expectation, all reason. It changed me. I would never be the same after this. <i>We</i> would never be the same after this.</b><br><br>I do have to throw in some positive, though. I never am this harsh and even with that harsh reality of how I really felt about this book, there were still moments that made me smile and reminisce. The absolute best scene(s) in this story was when the shit hit the fan. Oh yeah, you all know that part-when everything falls apart. THAT was the most emotion I felt in the whole novel. Pretty much anything that happened to do with the unraveling of it all was the best. I cried a little for the airport scene and I felt pain when Kiera realized what she'd done....to everyone. It was just...it was everything I had wanted for the whole book-too bad it was so late in the story. I loved being in his head for just for the simple fact of how and why he does what he does with other women. It was touching in a way I never imagined possible, because I felt like it would be hard to read about him having sex with other women, but it was okay, for me, because I saw what it did for him. It was about that one moment of connection and how it made him feel alive, wanted, complacent...if only until his climax when he is discarded just like he does with his condoms. It was heartbreaking. But, on that same token, if you don't want to see the illustrious Kellan Kyle have sex with someone besides Kiera-this book isn't for you. <br><br><b>Maybe what we'd done was wrong, but we'd loved with all our hearts, and no one could take that away from us. Not Denny, not fate, not life.</b><br><br>So, to all my friends who have been asking me if they should read this? No. I do NOT recommend this book if you held the <i>Thoughtless</i> series dear to your heart, like I did. For those who just want more Kellan? Go for it. And for those who don't mind monotonous accounts of his everyday life as he waits to see Kiera again, filler scenes that feel dull and lifeless, generally repetitive thoughts and accounts of what had already happened, and shameless obsession (we know he loved her to the point of obsession, but seeing it play out and just knowing it by our own knowledge is completely different. It ruins it when we're forced to hear it every page) that makes you feel just plain sorry for him...then this is your book. <br><br>There will always be nostalgia with this story and I will always get those little butterflies-But it wasn't what the story could be. S.C. Stephens-you sold yourself short....and I'm so damn sad.<br><br><br><i>**ARC kindly provided by Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br><br><br><br>For more of my reviews, please visit:<br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491628712i/22430034._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>
</u><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/%20" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="60" width="139" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409285880i/10960212.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>
</u><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>*******************************************************<br><br><br><b>Wellll...something amazing has happened.</b> It seems fate has reached out and decided FOR ME whether to read this or not-while I am STILL super nervous to read this book that could potentially ruin one of my all time favorite series ever, <b>I have been given an ARC!!!!!!</b> So, it seems, that I am about to read a book I am very apprehensive about....but also so excited about that I might pee my pants. So, eh, I've never been that smart anyway. lol.<br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/complicated_zps134dfd6a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415283303ra/11764117.gif" alt=" photo complicated_zps134dfd6a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>*****************************************<br><br><b>To read, or not to read??</b><br><br>I don't know yet. I have seen this bouncing around on GR and I don't know if I can put myself through another FAILED male POV. Do I take the chance and possibly ruin one of my all time favorite series....? Or just leave it be as is and accept that I was happy enough with the story as Stephens left it. <br><br>After the massacre also known as <b>WALKING DISASTER</b> (Which irrevocably changed my feelings and ruined my outlook about one of my other all time favorites Beautiful Disaster) I am skeptical as to whether I'm willing to put the Thoughtless series at risk. <br><br>But Stephens is a better author than McGuire.....so I'm still 50/50. Guess we'll see. <br><br><br>******OH! Another example of an epic fail in Male POV is <b>Come Alive</b> by Karina Halle. It ALMOST ruined my outlook on the series....but book 8 came back strong and became another favorite of mine....</span>
  <a data-text-id="15676894012700015974" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823400898?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823400898" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5565057031927677793"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 "Mornin'" STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425102098i/13845801._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>♫♪“He knows that I'm a friend of yours, but doesn't know I've crossed the line.<br/>I know you've got a man in the picture, but it hasn't stopped me yet.<br/>We've all been in one situation or another we regret.<br/><br/>Now I'm the other man, no one's rootin' for me.<br/>If I'm the other man, nature will abhor me.<br/>To be the other man, no one's sympathizes.<br/>When you're the other man that everyone despises.<br/><br/>He's going to find out that the rumo</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5565057031927677793" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 "Mornin'" STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425102098i/13845801._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>♫♪“He knows that I'm a friend of yours, but doesn't know I've crossed the line.<br>I know you've got a man in the picture, but it hasn't stopped me yet.<br>We've all been in one situation or another we regret.<br><br>Now I'm the other man, no one's rootin' for me.<br>If I'm the other man, nature will abhor me.<br>To be the other man, no one's sympathizes.<br>When you're the other man that everyone despises.<br><br>He's going to find out that the rumours are true.<br>The love that I've still unbeknownst to you.”♪♫ <br><br><i><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eIQzRogbMZw" rel="nofollow noopener"> Sloan - The Other Man</a></i><br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410228282i/11077080._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I don’t want to feel guilty about something that makes me feel so…whole.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Oh, how I missed Kellan dearly! And getting his POV was awesome and very emotional. I'm not going to lie, I was really worried <br>about reading this. I have read books before where the same story is being told in the alternate POV, and I have not enjoyed it. I love Kellan a lot, since he was one of my first book boyfriends ever, I didn't want to be disappointed by his book. I am glad to say that it did not, at all. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I knew I was overstepping so many boundaries right now that it was ridiculous, but I couldn't help myself. Holding her—just holding her—felt better than anything I’d felt in a while.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>If you have read <i>Thoughtless</i>, then you are very aware what this book is about. Yes, we get the exact same story, but the writing was so wonderfully done that I was able to feel of the intense angst and emotion the Kellan Kyle suffered. It really was almost like a new experience and not at all like you were reading the same thing over again. I knew what would happen next, but that didn't stop me from connecting to the story. I loved knowing all of his thoughts, when he felt love, hatred, and sadness. Reading about his vulnerable moments first hand was completely heart breaking. I teared up a lot during those moments. I also felt all of that frustration from seeing the direction Kellan and Keira's relationship was headed.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425102186ra/13845810.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>'You begged me to stay. You cried for me. You made love to me. How can I possibly leave you alone after that? When I love you more than anything else in this world? I just want a part of you, is that too much to ask?<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Not everything that was in this book was the same as <i>Thoughtless</i>. Here, we get a better insight into Kellan's horrible childhood. We also get to see how Kellan and Denny's friendship began. I appreciated seeing that, I also appreciated the fact that we get a better understanding of Denny's actions, as well. I don't know how S.C. Stephens did it, but she managed to make the same story feel brand new and different. This had me bawling just like the Keira's book. Overall, I really enjoyed this book. It had an overload of angst, as did the first. It made me angry and so upset, but it also made smile so big and fall in love with Kellan all over again. I loved every moment of this book. I could not put it down. I definitely recommend this one to you angst lovers and of course to those who love Kellan Kyle.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410228282i/11077080._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5565057031927677793" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/820586618" />
    <a title="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10312276-melissa-mel-reader"><img alt="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517366723p2/10312276.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/820586618?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" href="/user/show/10312276-melissa-mel-reader">MELISSA *Mel Reader*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer820586618" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12090903553611771025"><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.facebook.com/SCStephensAuthor/app_601644833234446'>https://www.facebook.com/SCStephensAu...</a><br/><br/>Merged review:<br/><br/>4 "You Mean Everything To Me" Stars!<br/>(BR with Patty & Sharon)<br/><br/><i>
  <b>I felt more comfortable in the spotlight than I felt being alone.</b>
</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/fa80fa6b-fd95-4235-b7f6-91a4c1c7b289_zpsftf78ysu.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424887469i/13815326.jpg' alt=' photo fa80fa6b-fd95-4235-b7f6-91a4c1c7b289_zpsftf78ysu.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>In Thoughtful we get Kellan's side & everything he was feeling. I liked his POV & finding out how gone he was over Kiera from the beginning. We also get more of his past with his family & how worthless and unloveable they made him feel growing up. We get more from his past with Denny too & how they bonded like b</span>
  <span id="freeText12090903553611771025" style="display:none"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SCStephensAuthor/app_601644833234446">https://www.facebook.com/SCStephensAu...</a><br><br>Merged review:<br><br>4 "You Mean Everything To Me" Stars!<br>(BR with Patty &amp; Sharon)<br><br><i>
  <b>I felt more comfortable in the spotlight than I felt being alone.</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/fa80fa6b-fd95-4235-b7f6-91a4c1c7b289_zpsftf78ysu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424887469i/13815326.jpg" alt=" photo fa80fa6b-fd95-4235-b7f6-91a4c1c7b289_zpsftf78ysu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In Thoughtful we get Kellan's side &amp; everything he was feeling. I liked his POV &amp; finding out how gone he was over Kiera from the beginning. We also get more of his past with his family &amp; how worthless and unloveable they made him feel growing up. We get more from his past with Denny too &amp; how they bonded like brothers from the start. We see how desperate Kellan was for a connection with someone &amp; that he just wanted to feel wanted. He didn't think love was something he could ever have until Kiera. <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/3ed73108-4b9d-4549-87ee-5bb961654cf0_zpsnezpw1kd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424888061i/13815458.jpg" alt=" photo 3ed73108-4b9d-4549-87ee-5bb961654cf0_zpsnezpw1kd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>I simply stared at her and thanked whatever fates there were for bringing her into my life.</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/ac977f40-c98f-4380-b1a0-e6f1a322bf4f_zps3xxyz9bs.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425942549i/13953082.jpg" alt=" photo ac977f40-c98f-4380-b1a0-e6f1a322bf4f_zps3xxyz9bs.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>There was a connection between us, something beyond just physical attraction.</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/fdffd1e0-0881-46f1-8a41-bc7e40cc7995_zpsigvp55ql.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425240126i/13866323.jpg" alt=" photo fdffd1e0-0881-46f1-8a41-bc7e40cc7995_zpsigvp55ql.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>She was everything I wanted, everything I needed, everything I hoped for.</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/9d64c53f-335d-43bc-b220-ae8f2ef36390_zpsrw7d0y10.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425945434i/13953336.jpg" alt=" photo 9d64c53f-335d-43bc-b220-ae8f2ef36390_zpsrw7d0y10.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>My heart was Kiera's alone. Fully and completely.</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/6ca39ecf-4839-4605-8819-798319fc71b9_zpscoc7ch0q.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425945434i/13953337._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6ca39ecf-4839-4605-8819-798319fc71b9_zpscoc7ch0q.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
