<div id="review_1208974906" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1208974906" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1208974906?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1208974906" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2999807064385974538"><b>★★★ 3.5 stars ★★★</b><br/><br/><b>Please don't hate me before you read this review….</b><br/><br/>One thing that was evident when I started reading <i>Thoughtful</i> is that I don't, or I didn't, understand Kellan Kyle near as well as I thought I did. So far, we have gotten Kellan's explanation (through Kiera's POV) as to why his lifestyle was filled with meaningless sex, music, and more meaningless sex. His past dialogue has enlightened us to why he <i>needed</i> those women, that connection. However, it wasn't until this book that I trul</span>
  <span id="freeText2999807064385974538" style="display:none"><b>★★★ 3.5 stars ★★★</b><br /><br /><b>Please don't hate me before you read this review….</b><br /><br />One thing that was evident when I started reading <i>Thoughtful</i> is that I don't, or I didn't, understand Kellan Kyle near as well as I thought I did. So far, we have gotten Kellan's explanation (through Kiera's POV) as to why his lifestyle was filled with meaningless sex, music, and more meaningless sex. His past dialogue has enlightened us to why he <i>needed</i> those women, that connection. However, it wasn't until this book that I truly understood it, and that understanding starts from the very first page. It connected me with Kellan in a way that the other books just couldn't. <br /><br />So, as a long time (pink cover free version long time) fan of this series, reading <i>Thoughtful</i> was a true gift.<br /><br />The reason I didn't rate it higher is that this book just didn't quite carry the same punch as <i>Thoughtless</i>. However, the impossibility of being able to do that is not the author's fault. We get to see some flashbacks from Kellan's POV and a few scenes from when Kellan wasn't with Kiera, but for the most part, this follows the same storyline and progression of events as <i>Thoughtless</i>. The emotions I felt when first reading this series from Kiera's POV were impossible to duplicate with the same intensity. It was also hard not to skim certain parts that seemed to move a little slower in order to get to one of those more memorable/pivotal scenes, but I'm glad she stayed on point with <i>Thoughtless</i>. If she hadn't, there's a possibility that one of the scenes that I had personally been dying to read might not have been included. I got what I wanted. This makes me happy.<br /><br />One of my absolute favorite things about this book happens to be one of my not so favorites. What can I say, I'm controversial. In <i>Thoughtful</i>, we are introduced to a totally new Kellan Kyle. His love and infatuation with Kiera is palpable. His sensitivity, full of passion, but I didn't get to see much more than that. Kellan's defense mechanism is protecting his emotions with a thick layer of confidence and flirtiness, and sometimes mixed with a little asshole. I know much of this is a front, but I believe with all of my heart that <s>my</s> our Kellan Kyle shares some of the same characteristics he shows on the surface. When he's on stage, he radiates strength, sexuality, confidence and a lot of testosterone, but we don't see much of that below the surface in <i>Thoughtful</i>. I loved the emotional side of Kellan, but I feel this book lost the, for lack of a better word, manlier (and sometimes playful) side. I loved so much getting to discover a new Kellan, one I didn't really know before, but I missed seeing the one that I thought I already knew.<br /><br />I don't want anyone to take this review as me saying I didn't enjoy the book. It is a great companion to this series, a series that is so high on my shelf of favorites that I don't even think I can reach it anymore. When you love a book and a author's work as much as I do the this series and S.C. Stephens, more is <i>always</i> a good thing. The scenes this book contains from Kellan's POV are invaluable and even though it may have contained some things I didn't like, imperfections are irrelevant with unconditional love and this series has definitely earned that. <br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br /><b>Check out the <i>Thoughtful</i> book trailer:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HraQw-5OkCI">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HraQw...</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2999807064385974538" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1166721911" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1166721911" />
    <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog"><img alt="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514886578p2/7379751.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1166721911?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog">Gitte TotallyBookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1166721911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10322367487308557778"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421366246i/13367072._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>5++ EMOTIONAL STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><br/><b> ‘I would never be the same after this. We would never be the same after this.’</b><br/><br/><br/>We’ll start by saying if you haven’t already done so; we strongly suggest reading Thoughtless <b>before</b> reading this book. Although set in the same timeframe, reading Thoughtful will allow you to experience the shift in this story told from Kellan’s perspective. And secondly……Arrrrggghhh this book! <b>Our hearts!</b> We are exhausted! Emotionally wrung out!<br/><br/><br/><b>‘I wrapped my fury around me like armor. Let her t</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10322367487308557778" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421366246i/13367072._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>5++ EMOTIONAL STARS!!!</b><br><br><br><b> ‘I would never be the same after this. We would never be the same after this.’</b><br><br><br>We’ll start by saying if you haven’t already done so; we strongly suggest reading Thoughtless <b>before</b> reading this book. Although set in the same timeframe, reading Thoughtful will allow you to experience the shift in this story told from Kellan’s perspective. And secondly……Arrrrggghhh this book! <b>Our hearts!</b> We are exhausted! Emotionally wrung out!<br><br><br><b>‘I wrapped my fury around me like armor. Let her try to find a crack. I dared her.’</b><br><br><br>We’ll be honest. We were a bit nervous when we heard Thoughtful was in the works. Kellan was, and still is, one of our <b>favourite book boyfriends</b> with the Thoughtless series being forever embedded in our hearts. It goes without saying too much of Kellan is never enough, but still, we had concerns.<br><br><br>Firstly, we knew Kellan’s story would be painful. We <b>felt his pain, loneliness and confusion</b> enough in Thoughtless, hearing it from Kellan first hand was definitely going to be difficult and would add a new dimension to Thoughtless that we weren’t sure we were prepared for.<br><br><br><b>‘Being in love was so hard. But not being in love was even worse.’</b><br><br><br>Another concern was this being the same book from a different perspective. It’s been done before and in some cases it’s worked brilliantly by enhancing the original story, yet in others it’s damaged the original story beyond repair. We know SC Stephens is a brilliant storyteller who evokes strong emotions in her words and that she fervently loves her characters, but nonetheless there was a part of us that worried this book could fall in the latter and that would have broken our hearts.<br><br><br><b>‘It was so hard to see her in pain. It was even harder to know I was the source of it. I was tormenting her, she said so herself.’</b><br><br><br>But we<b> HAD</b> to delve in and we’re thrilled to say Thoughtful definitely fell into the former, as <b>Kellan’s POV positively enhanced</b> what was already one of our all-time favourite books. It felt fresh, new and gave us insights that had us aching, smiling and <b>falling love with Kellan</b> and this book all over again! <br><br><br><b>‘I was not about to give her the satisfaction of seeing my pain. My emotional pain anyway. That was mine, she didn’t have a right to it.’</b><br><br><br>Told from Kellan’s perspective his words were heartbreaking, passionate and highly emotional. Kellan wears his heart on his sleeve and we felt, lived and breathed everything Kellan went through. The depth of his anger, frustration, confusion and love, his unexpected feelings for Kiera, <b>WE! FELT! EVERYTHING!</b> Deep in our hearts.<br><br><br><b>‘I knew, without a doubt in my head, that I could fall asleep with her in my arms every night and be completely happy. And that thought, scared the crap out of me, because on the flip side, I knew I would be completely miserable without her.’</b><br><br><br>There’s no doubting this relationship was toxic not only to themselves but those around them and through Kellan’s eyes we really experienced that aspect of the story.<br><br><br><b>‘The three of us all living together could be an incredible, eye-opening experience. Or it could be a living nightmare. Either way, it was definitely going to be interesting.’</b><br><br><br>We’ve been asked by readers if this book is merely a rehash?” Our answer is <b>NO</b>, it most certainly didn’t feel that way to us at all. Sure, parts of dialogue are carried through from Thoughtless but they are brought about in a new light making them feel very new and different in Thoughtful. SC Stephens has also explored and expanded scenes and delved into the dynamics of Kellan’s other relationships besides his and Kiera’s making Thoughtful such an enlightening experience.<br><br><br>The relationships with Kellan and Denny, and Kellan and the band were fleshed out in Thoughtful, and in particular Kellan’s relationship with Evan was something we really enjoyed. We knew these two had a bond, but the depth of that bond was so heart-warming.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t let her go, Evan. I tried. I tried to stay away, I tried to forget her.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>The relationship between Denny and Kellan is also one which SC Stephens took to another level in Thoughtful. This time around we really felt the brotherhood between these two men, making the utter betrayal and hurt Kiera and Kellan caused Denny all the more painful to experience.<br><br><br><b>‘I’d wanted her, so I’d taken her. I was no friend to him, to anyone. ‘</b><br><br><br>Although we all knew the outcome, the journey to the final destination in Thoughtful felt new and different allowing us to really feel what was going through Kellan’s head throughout this tumultuous and passionate relationship.<br><br><br><b>‘If she was going to be a bitch, then I would be her bastard.’</b><br><br><br>We’ve no doubt fans of this series are going to <b>love this book.</b> It really does offer up a new level to the original story and through it all we felt the gut wrenching <b>agony,</b> the <b>anger</b>, the <b>hurt</b>, the joy, the loss, the <b>passion and the absolute love</b> experienced by this man upon finding his soulmate. <b>**WARNING: Have tissues at the ready!!</b> You’ll need them…we did!!! Prepare to let Kellan Kyle steal your heart all over again. Oh Kellan….sigh….you have our hearts buddy!<br><br><br><i>**Reviewed from an ARC copy provided by Grand Central Publishing, with thanks.’<br>***Please note: Quotes may/may not be included in final release***</i><br><br><br><a href="http://wp.me/p2WbFf-37" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review of Thoughtless - Book One</a><br><a href="http://wp.me/p2WbFf-2r" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review of Effortless- Book Two </a><br><a href="http://wp.me/p2WbFf-1y8" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review of Reckless Book Three</a><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>✦✦&lt; TB Blog :<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦✦✦ Come say Hi : <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦✦✦Follow us: <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦✦✦Check out: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a> <br>✦✦✦ We're on TSU: <a href="https://www.tsu.co/TBBLOG" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on TSU</a></span>

<div id="review_823346097" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823346097?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823346097" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13034714394137423636"><b>Holy shit!! I can't wait! </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413444597i/11511236._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='570' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Kellan, I have missed you!!<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413461784i/11513196.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Shhh...don't tell my hubby ;)<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413461937ra/11513223.gif' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/></span>
  <span id="freeText13034714394137423636" style="display:none"><b>Holy shit!! I can't wait! </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413444597i/11511236._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="570" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kellan, I have missed you!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413461784i/11513196.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Shhh...don't tell my hubby ;)<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413461937ra/11513223.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_823390567" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/823390567" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412857185p2/13978199.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823390567?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review">arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=dying-to-get-my-hands-on">dying-to-get-my-hands-on</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=angsty-romance">angsty-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=fav-books-of-all-time">fav-books-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=rock-stars">rock-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823390567" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14856721771881186284">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br/><br/>5+++++ <b> “Mornin’” <i> “It’s better to never say goodbye, to just move on, to end the lie.” </i> “She was mine” </b> Kisses<br/><br/>I don’t know how to talk about this series without putting my whole heart on paper…that’s how much I love it. The Thoughtless series is one of my favorite series of all time…one of my top three BBF’s of all time…one of my favorite couples ever…it means <i>so</i> much to me that even contemplating putting my feelings about it into words makes me tear up – it</span>
  <span id="freeText14856721771881186284" style="display:none">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br><br>5+++++ <b> “Mornin’” <i> “It’s better to never say goodbye, to just move on, to end the lie.” </i> “She was mine” </b> Kisses<br><br>I don’t know how to talk about this series without putting my whole heart on paper…that’s how much I love it. The Thoughtless series is one of my favorite series of all time…one of my top three BBF’s of all time…one of my favorite couples ever…it means <i>so</i> much to me that even contemplating putting my feelings about it into words makes me tear up – it just has that hold over my heart. I was really nervous going into <i>Thoughtful</i> because I <b>needed</b> it to be amazing…I’ve been dying to get into Kellan Kyle’s head for almost 2 ½ years...a lot was on the line. Well my thoughts, hopes, dreams and any and all expectations were completely and totally blown out of the water. <i>Thoughtful</i> was everything I could have imagined and then some…love doesn’t even begin to cover how I feel about this book. In case you haven’t read the Thoughtless series or met the god that is Kellan Kyle…then please stop immediately and go read <i>Thoughtless</i>…like, right now. This is a series that absolutely <b>must</b> be read in order and while you can read <i>Effortless</i> and <i>Reckless</i>before <i> Thoughtful</i>, you <b>have</b> to read <i>Thoughtless</i> first.<br><br>Kellan Kyle…the rock star…the sex god…the man defies explanation. I knew from the very beginning there was so much untapped potential…so much promise behind those beautiful blue eyes…and actually knowing and understanding him a little better has finally given my heart peace. It’s not that Kellan never opened up in <i>Thoughtless</i>…he does…but hearing them tell someone their thoughts and feelings and reading everything straight from the character…it’s just two different things. There is absolutely no filter between Kellan and me and there is no way to fully express how deeply I felt everything he was saying. I <i>knew</i> it was going to be hard…I <i>knew</i> it was going to hurt but I did not come close to how incredible it <b>actually</b> was. It was like falling in love with him all over again. I found a new, deeper appreciation for this brilliant character that I already thought was amazing.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424867810i/13811987._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘When we pulled into the driveway, I shut the car off and looked down at Kiera sleeping on me. She seemed so comfortable, so content. I wanted to stroke her hair, cup her cheek, kiss her forehead. A surging desire was building in me to put both my arms around her and hold her tight. To tell her how much she meant to me, that no one saw me the way she did, no one cared for me the way she did. To tell her I cared about her in a way that sometimes scared the crap out of me. She was comfort and pain, wrapped up in one beautiful package…that wasn’t mine.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Kiera Allen…I have always had this love for Kiera that I cannot explain. I never hated her…I may have been frustrated with her – and seeing her actions through Kellan’s eyes didn’t change that…but on some level, I understood what she was going through. I didn’t envy her decision or her struggle…she’s faced with the impossible choice…her first love, the only man that she has ever been with and a guy that represents a huge part of her life….or this amazing man that lights her up and makes her feel things she’s never experienced before. I understood and saw her fear and reluctance for what it was. I think <i>really</i> knowing how Kellan felt about her and seeing her from his POV almost made everything that they went through worth it…because I have a new found appreciation for what her presence did to him and for him. It’s really hard to explain and I really feel like it’s something that needs to be experienced…in the moment…hearing it straight from Kellan…I just get it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424867810i/13811988._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> “Don’t do this,” I whispered to myself between our hungry lips. <i>This will only hurt us…all three of us. Be strong enough to walk away. Stop this.</i> Her lips pressed harder against mine. Even as pain leached out of my throat in a whimper, my willpower dissolved. “What are you doing, Kiera?” <i>What am I doing?</i><br>She paused with her lips brushing mine. “I don’t know…just don’t leave me, please don’t leave me.” The truth and pain in her voice were undeniable – <i>she wanted me.</i><br>Her eyes were shut, so she couldn’t see the smile on my face. <i>I won’t. I won’t ever leave you.</i> “Kiera…please…” <i>I’m yours…take me.</i> My resistance faded away with a shudder, and I sought her mouth. I needed her. I’d always needed her. And she wanted me to stay…she wanted me with her…she wanted me. And I was hers.’ </b> </blockquote><br>My love for Kellan and Kiera might be at an all time high right now…their story, their feelings for each other…from beginning to end, I can’t help but love every single ounce of these two. They’re so alike and yet so different in so many ways, but the one thing they have is this unending desire to be with each other…just being around the other makes them more complete and I love that <b>so</b> much. It’s always been more about their emotional connection than anything else between these two and <i>Thoughtless</i> really showed me that. The joy that was brought to my heart with every time they held hands or he made her laugh or blush or when she would talk to him about his music…that’s just all I need in life. I’m a stickler for one thing…repetitiveness…I hate it. I can handle it in small doses, but if it gets to be too much then I start to disconnect. This is the same story as <i>Thoughtless</i>…so you would think the repetitiveness of reading the same story would drive me crazy – it did not <i>feel</i> like the same story. Every emotion and detail I was reading was fresh and new…and even though I knew exactly what was going to happen next, I was still holding my breath with each click of my kindle.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424867810ra/13811989.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘She seemed amused by that. “Eventually you’re going to start making sense, right?”<br>I laughed and looked out over the skyline, “Yeah…just give me a minute.” Or three, or four. <i>I can do this…</i><br>Respecting my wishes, Kiera put her head on my shoulder and held me tight. As I held her head in place and rubbed her back, I felt my unease dissolving. This wasn’t just anyone I was opening up to. This was Kiera. She had my heart, every corner of it, so what did it matter if she knew about the darkness that surrounded me? She would love me anyway. I was sure of that. My secrets were safe with her. I was safe with her.’ </b> </blockquote><br>I don’t know why hearing the same story from a different POV affected me differently…but it did. I <b>know</b> their story…the order of events isn’t different but the emotional impact that is had on me is 1000000000% a new experience. Understanding Kellan’s thoughts and feelings…seeing things from a new perspective…getting facts that weren’t exactly as clear the first time around…it was like reading <i>Thoughtless</i> for the first time. And <b>god</b> did that book gut me the first time around but for whatever reason I didn’t know if I was going to survive it from Kellan’s POV. The rawness of his emotions was something I don’t experience very often. Maybe it’s because he’s one of my favorites, maybe it’s because I love this story so much – I really don’t care the reason why it hit me so hard because it was the most exquisite pain and I couldn’t help but love every second of it. I feel like <i>Thoughtful</i> brought a new clarity to a character that is so deeply rooted in my heart, I never will forget him…and getting this insight on him was worth every second of pain…it made me appreciate him and love him more than I thought possible.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424867810ra/13811990.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> “I love you.”<br>The words were so simple, a barely speaking child could learn them, but they were so damn powerful….lives had been destroyed because of them. And their effect on me was immediate. My eyes burned as moisture worked its way to the surface. I shut them and twin tears worked their way down my cheeks. I felt like sobbing. I felt like laughing. Joy and pain spun around within me in an agonizing dance, and I had no idea which emotion was in the lead. <i>She does love me. Someone loves me.</i><br>I felt Kiera brush my tears aside. “I love you…so much.” </b> </blockquote><br>Another reason I loved it…it made me love the D-Bags even more. Of course seeing them through Kiera’s eyes it’s impossible not to fall for these guys and their little band bro-mance they have…it’s an amazing combination and brings light and humor to an angsty series…but really understanding the friendship that they have with Kellan…it’s just one more layer than I couldn’t help but adore. Especially the Kellan/Evan relationship…that was kind of an awesome surprise. I mean…I knew Evan was a great guy but it’s not like I remember any of their conversations being that impactful, but this time around, I had a new found admiration for the way Evan helped and support Kellan. Something I was excited to see and really enjoyed understanding more was the way Kellan and Denny handled everything that happened. It’s no secret how much Kellan thought of Denny and how conflicted he was over damaging that relationship…and we get the basics on how everything goes after the fight…but I did feel like I got more out of that. The whole situation is messy but they’re all trying to make the best of it…and I appreciated getting more insight into what happened between the two of them. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402787212ra/9986745.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘The memory of who I was before she came into my life, exactly a year ago, pounded through my brain – the loneliness, the desperation to connect – I couldn’t go back to that emptiness. I wouldn’t survive it. “I don’t want to be alone anymore,” I muttered, barely conscious of saying it. <i>I don’t want to be without you anymore. Ever. ’ </i> </b> </blockquote><br>It’s funny because while I was reading…and loving every second…I had the same feels that I did with <i>Thoughtless</i>. I wanted it to be over and never end in the same breath…it’s very conflicting and confusing…but it works. Now that I have a taste of KK’s mind…I want <b>more</b>! This shouldn’t be a surprise…I’m a Stage 5 Clinger and if there is anyone I cling to the most, it’s Kellan Kyle…but he’s like a drug that I will never stop being addicted to. Am I content with getting <i>Thoughtful</i>…of course I am…but I would <b>gladly</b> accept <i>Effortless</i> and <i>Reckless</i> from KK’s POV. Because…more Kellan is always amazing. :-)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424867810i/13811991._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874066.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14856721771881186284" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1157690895" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15163665470629349734"><b>4 'I Like cream in my coffee' Stars</b><br/><br/>We all know by now who Kellan Kyle is by now. If you don't...where have you been? what the hell is wrong with you? I suggest you go read it ASAP. Don't even bother reading this review, just go, leave, bye, Adios.<br/><br/><b>Spoilers ahead</b><br/><br/>*takes a deep breath* <br/><br/>So ladies and gentleman, please round an applause for <b> Kellan-Fucking-Kyle</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpskytsjhz5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425681874i/13916451._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zpskytsjhz5.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>You might know him from <i>Thoughtless</i> and from the band the "D-bags". Yeah I know cool name. So long story short is...Kellan is friends with </span>
  <span id="freeText15163665470629349734" style="display:none"><b>4 'I Like cream in my coffee' Stars</b><br><br>We all know by now who Kellan Kyle is by now. If you don't...where have you been? what the hell is wrong with you? I suggest you go read it ASAP. Don't even bother reading this review, just go, leave, bye, Adios.<br><br><b>Spoilers ahead</b><br><br>*takes a deep breath* <br><br>So ladies and gentleman, please round an applause for <b> Kellan-Fucking-Kyle</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpskytsjhz5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425681874i/13916451._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpskytsjhz5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You might know him from <i>Thoughtless</i> and from the band the "D-bags". Yeah I know cool name. So long story short is...Kellan is friends with Danny who decided to move in and be roommates but Danny is not moving in alone he and his girlfriend Kiera are both gonna be roommates with my boogy-boo Kellan, Danny has to go on a trip for a job, shit happens which ends up bad kiera is mad so she fucks Kellan then Danny comes home and fucks her then that's when shit goes down people...brace yourself cause its gonna be a wild ride.<br><br><b>“Friend. Lover. Companion. Family”</b><br><br>This book was just like thoughtless but in Kellan's pov. And get this straight, the pain only gets worse. Now I get to know how Kellan felt and I'll tell you this, I still got mad at Keira. She would annoy me in thoughtless and she still annoys me now. I couldn't read this book straight, I had to take breaks from all the pain that Kellan and I both faced. And come on Keira "Just Friends" you know those never work. <br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps9dahem8b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425681874i/13916452._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps9dahem8b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cause it will lead to this....<br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsowwdxofd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425681874i/13916453.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsowwdxofd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then this...<br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsklwpuvgz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425681874i/13916454.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsklwpuvgz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And I still felt bad for Danny. Even after everything I still like him and the were just playing fire with fire.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsfpy7jwjq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425681874i/13916455._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsfpy7jwjq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Overall it was amazing to go inside Kellan's head even though it was painful.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpszqc2keir.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425681874i/13916456._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpszqc2keir.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>BTW I'm I the only one who finds it funny and cute that the cover for this book is him and his "baby". I sometimes actually liked their relationship better than when he's with Kiera.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15163665470629349734" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xAUb3T2OpCUueZ8VhHKjlUsLxpDJEfQmgoFjul9F7OxCVsl36oSZ3G0BPzyDQ8noWngBMK7dv8sjBPjXYUcnqA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1y+eBUkmNuSyUClG6UdfJDxbQQGwxRYMEEIE/D+6ee1RfEyvniwLHfEoiW/udjVZLSiGodcJXeGxx5+RAbiyqQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7386068351062809043">S.C. Stephens is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author who enjoys spending every free moment she has creating stories that are packed with emotion and heavy on romance. <br/><br/>Her debut novel, Thoughtless, an angst-filled love triangle charged with insurmountable passion and the unforgettable Kellan Kyle, took the literary world by storm. Amazed and surprised by the response to the release of</span>
  <span id="freeText7386068351062809043" style="display:none">S.C. Stephens is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author who enjoys spending every free moment she has creating stories that are packed with emotion and heavy on romance. <br /><br />Her debut novel, Thoughtless, an angst-filled love triangle charged with insurmountable passion and the unforgettable Kellan Kyle, took the literary world by storm. Amazed and surprised by the response to the release of Thoughtless in 2009, more stories were quick to follow. Stephens has been writing nonstop ever since.<br /><br />In addition to writing, Stephens enjoys spending lazy afternoons in the sun reading fabulous novels, loading up her iPod with writer's block reducing music, heading out to the movies, and spending quality time with her friends and family. She currently resides in the beautiful Pacific Northwest with her two equally beautiful children.<br /><br /></span>

    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>
